    pub type Reference<T> = Rc<RefCell<T>>;
    pub type ConstReference<T> = Rc<T>;
    pub type WeakReference<T> = Weak<RefCell<T>>;

    pub fn build_ref<T>(value: T) -> Reference<T> {
        Rc::new(RefCell::new(value))
    }
    pub fn build_const_ref<T>(value: T) -> ConstReference<T> {
        Rc::new(value)
    }
    pub fn clone_ref<T>(value: &Reference<T>) -> Reference<T> {
        Rc::clone(value)
    }
    pub fn clone_const_ref<T>(value: &ConstReference<T>) -> ConstReference<T> {
        Rc::clone(value)
    }
    pub fn clone_weak_ref<T>(value: &Reference<T>) -> WeakReference<T> {
        Rc::downgrade(&value)
    }
    pub fn print_type_of<T>(_: &T) -> &'static str {
        std::any::type_name::<T>()
    }
    pub struct Timer {
        timestep: Instant,
        name: String,
    }
    impl Timer {
        pub fn new(name: &str) -> Self {
            {
                ::std::io::_print(format_args!("Timer \'{0}\' started.\n", name));
            };
            Timer {
                timestep: Instant::now(),
                name: name.to_string(),
            }
        }
        pub fn reset(&mut self) {
            self.timestep = Instant::now();
        }
        pub fn elapsed(&self) -> u128 {
            self.timestep.elapsed().as_millis()
        }
        pub fn report(&self) {
            {
                ::std::io::_print(
                    format_args!(
                        "Timer \'{0}\' elapsed time: {1:.2?}ms.\n",
                        self.name,
                        self.elapsed(),
                    ),
                );
            };
        }
    }
    impl Drop for Timer {
        fn drop(&mut self) {
            self.report();
        }
    }
    pub fn exit() {
        std::process::exit(0);
    }
    pub struct ListMap<K, V> {
        list: Vec<Reference<V>>,
        map: Dict<K, (usize, Reference<V>)>,
    }
    impl<K, V: fmt::Debug> fmt::Debug for ListMap<K, V> {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.write_fmt(format_args!("ListMap {0:#?}", self.list))
        }
    }
    impl<K: Eq + Hash, V> Default for ListMap<K, V> {
        fn default() -> Self {
            ListMap {
                list: Vec::new(),
                map: Dict::new(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl<K: Eq + Hash, V> ListMap<K, V> {
        pub fn push(&mut self, key: K, value: V) {
            self.list.push(build_ref(value));
            self.map
                .insert(key, (self.list.len() - 1, self.list.last().unwrap().clone()));
        }
        pub fn get(&self, key: &K) -> Option<&Reference<V>> {
            self.map.get(key).map(|(_, v)| v)
        }
        pub fn get_mut(&mut self, key: &K) -> Option<&mut Reference<V>> {
            self.map.get_mut(key).map(|(_, v)| v)
        }
        pub fn index_of(&self, key: &K) -> usize {
            self.map.get(key).map(|(i, _)| *i).unwrap()
        }
        pub fn contains(&self, key: &K) -> bool {
            self.map.contains_key(key)
        }
        pub fn last(&self) -> Option<&Reference<V>> {
            self.list.last()
        }
        pub fn last_mut(&mut self) -> Option<&mut Reference<V>> {
            self.list.last_mut()
        }
        pub fn iter(&self) -> std::slice::Iter<Reference<V>> {
            self.list.iter()
        }
        pub fn len(&self) -> usize {
            self.list.len()
        }
        pub fn values(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Reference<V>> {
            self.list.iter()
        }
    }
    impl<K, V> Index<usize> for ListMap<K, V> {
        type Output = Reference<V>;
        fn index(&self, index: usize) -> &Self::Output {
            &self.list[index]
        }
    }
    impl<K: Eq + Hash, V> Index<&K> for ListMap<K, V> {
        type Output = Reference<V>;
        fn index(&self, key: &K) -> &Self::Output {
            self.get(key).unwrap()
        }
    }
    impl<K, V> IndexMut<usize> for ListMap<K, V> {
        fn index_mut(&mut self, index: usize) -> &mut Self::Output {
            &mut self.list[index]
        }
    }
    impl<K: Eq + Hash, V> IndexMut<&K> for ListMap<K, V> {
        fn index_mut(&mut self, key: &K) -> &mut Self::Output {
            self.get_mut(key).unwrap()
        }
    }
    pub fn norm1(p1: (float, float), p2: (float, float)) -> float {
        (p1.0 - p2.0).abs() + (p1.1 - p2.1).abs()
    }
    pub fn norm2(x1: float, y1: float, x2: float, y2: float) -> float {
        ((x1 - x2).powi(2) + (y1 - y2).powi(2)).sqrt()
    }
    pub fn change_path_suffix(path: &str, new_suffix: &str) -> String {
        let mut path_buf = PathBuf::from(path);
        if path_buf.set_extension(new_suffix) {
            path_buf.to_str().unwrap().to_string()
        } else {
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!("Failed to set the extension of the path."),
                );
            };
        }
    }
    pub fn fancy_index_1d<R: Clone, T: Clone + Copy + funty::Integral>(
        data: &Vec<R>,
        indices: &Vec<T>,
    ) -> Vec<R> {
        let mut result = Vec::with_capacity(indices.len());
        for &index in indices {
            result.push(data[index.as_usize()].clone());
        }
        result
    }
    pub fn fancy_index_2d<R: Clone, T: Clone + Copy + funty::Integral>(
        data: &Vec<Vec<R>>,
        row_indices: &Vec<T>,
        col_indices: &Vec<T>,
    ) -> Vec<Vec<R>> {
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        for &row in row_indices {
            let mut row_result = Vec::new();
            for &col in col_indices {
                row_result.push(data[row.as_usize()][col.as_usize()].clone());
            }
            result.push(row_result);
        }
        result
    }
    pub fn shape<T>(data: &Vec<Vec<T>>) -> (usize, usize) {
        (data.len(), data[0].len())
    }
    pub fn print_array_shape<T>(data: &[Vec<T>]) {
        {
            ::std::io::_print(
                format_args!("Shape: ({0}, {1})\n", data.len(), data[0].len()),
            );
        };
    }
    pub fn input() -> String {
        let mut input = String::new();
        io::stdin().read_line(&mut input).expect("Failed to read line");
        input.trim().to_string()
    }
    pub fn normalize_vector(vec: &mut Vec<f64>) {
        let magnitude = vec.iter().sum::<f64>();
        if magnitude > 0.0 {
            for element in vec.iter_mut() {
                *element /= magnitude;
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn cast_tuple<T: num::ToPrimitive, U: NumCast>(input: (T, T)) -> (U, U) {
        (U::from(input.0).unwrap(), U::from(input.1).unwrap())
    }
    pub fn natsorted(data: &mut Vec<String>) {
        data.sort_by(|a, b| natord::compare(a, b));
    }
    pub fn int_ceil_div<T: funty::Integral>(a: T, b: T) -> T {
        if !(a >= T::ZERO) {
            ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: a >= T::ZERO")
        }
        if !(b > T::ZERO) {
            ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: b > T::ZERO")
        }
        a / b + (if a % b > T::ZERO { T::ONE } else { T::ZERO })
    }
    pub fn redirect_output_to_null<F, T>(enable: bool, func: F) -> io::Result<T>
    where
        F: FnOnce() -> T,
    {
        if !enable {
            return Ok(func());
        }
        use std::os::unix::io::AsRawFd;
        let null = File::create("/dev/null")?;
        let stdout_fd = io::stdout().as_raw_fd();
        let stderr_fd = io::stderr().as_raw_fd();
        let stdout_backup = unsafe { libc::dup(stdout_fd) };
        let stderr_backup = unsafe { libc::dup(stderr_fd) };
        if stdout_backup == -1 || stderr_backup == -1 {
            return Err(io::Error::last_os_error());
        }
        unsafe {
            libc::dup2(null.as_raw_fd(), stdout_fd);
            libc::dup2(null.as_raw_fd(), stderr_fd);
        }
        let result = func();
        unsafe {
            libc::dup2(stdout_backup, stdout_fd);
            libc::dup2(stderr_backup, stderr_fd);
            libc::close(stdout_backup);
            libc::close(stderr_backup);
        }
        Ok(result)
    }
    pub fn format_float(num: f64, total_width: usize) -> String {
        if !(total_width > 0) {
            ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: total_width > 0")
        }
        let formatted = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                format_args!("{1:.0$e}", total_width - 1, num),
            );
            res
        });
        let formatted_num = formatted.parse::<f64>().unwrap_or(num);
        let precision = num.trunc().to_string().len() + 1;
        let total_width = formatted_num.to_string().len();
        if precision >= total_width {
            return ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("{0}", formatted_num));
                res
            });
        } else {
            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                    format_args!("{0:1$.2$}", num, total_width, total_width - precision),
                );
                res
            })
        }
    }
    /// Maps distance to a value between 0.0 and 1.0.
    /// Lower distance maps to higher value, and vice versa.
    ///
    /// Parameters:
    /// - distance: The input distance to map.
    /// - min_distance: The smallest expected distance (mapped to the highest value).
    /// - max_distance: The largest expected distance (mapped to the lowest value).
    ///
    /// Returns:
    /// - A value between 0.0 (lowest priority) and 1.0 (highest priority).
    pub fn map_distance_to_value<T: funty::Numeric + CCfloat>(
        distance: T,
        min_distance: T,
        max_distance: T,
    ) -> float {
        if !(distance >= min_distance) {
            {
                #[cold]
                #[track_caller]
                #[inline(never)]
                #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                }
                panic_cold_display(
                    &&::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "distance: {0}, min_distance: {1}",
                                distance,
                                min_distance,
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                );
            }
        }
        if !(distance <= max_distance) {
            {
                #[cold]
                #[track_caller]
                #[inline(never)]
                #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                }
                panic_cold_display(
                    &&::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "distance: {0}, max_distance: {1}",
                                distance,
                                max_distance,
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                );
            }
        }
        if min_distance == max_distance {
            return 1.0;
        }
        let distance = distance.float();
        let min_distance = min_distance.float();
        let max_distance = max_distance.float();
        let value = ((max_distance - distance) / (max_distance - min_distance));
        value
    }
    pub fn map_distances_to_values<
        T: funty::Numeric + CCfloat + ordered_float::FloatCore,
    >(distances: &Vec<T>) -> Vec<float> {
        let min_distance = distances
            .iter()
            .min_by_key(|x| OrderedFloat(**x))
            .unwrap()
            .clone();
        let max_distance = distances
            .iter()
            .max_by_key(|x| OrderedFloat(**x))
            .unwrap()
            .clone();
        distances
            .iter()
            .map(|&distance| map_distance_to_value(distance, min_distance, max_distance))
            .collect()
    }
    pub fn format_with_separator<T: CCf64>(n: T, sep: char) -> String {
        let n = n.f64();
        let n = round(n, 3);
        let integer_part = n.trunc() as i64;
        let formatted_integer = integer_part.to_string();
        let n_string = n.to_string();
        let formatted_decimal = if n_string.contains('.') {
            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                    format_args!(".{0}", &n_string.split('.').collect::<Vec<&str>>()[1]),
                );
                res
            })
        } else {
            "".to_string()
        };
        let mut formatted = String::new();
        let len = formatted_integer.len();
        for (i, c) in formatted_integer.chars().enumerate() {
            if i > 0 && (len - i) % 3 == 0 {
                formatted.push(sep);
            }
            formatted.push(c);
        }
        if formatted.len() <= 3 {
            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                    format_args!("{0}{1}", formatted, formatted_decimal),
                );
                res
            })
        } else {
            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("{0}", formatted));
                res
            })
        }
    }
    pub fn scientific_notation<T: CCf64>(n: T, precision: usize) -> String {
        let n = n.f64();
        if n == 0.0 {
            return "0".to_string();
        }
        let formatted = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("{0:.1$E}", n, precision));
            res
        });
        let parts: Vec<&str> = formatted.split('E').collect();
        let exponent: i32 = parts[1].parse().unwrap();
        let exp_str = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("{0:02}", exponent));
            res
        });
        let sign = if exponent >= 0 { "+" } else { "" };
        ::alloc::__export::must_use({
            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                format_args!("{0}E{1}{2}", parts[0], sign, exp_str),
            );
            res
        })
    }
    pub fn remove_postfix(file: &str) -> String {
        file.rsplit_once('.').map_or(file.to_string(), |(name, _)| name.to_string())
    }
    pub struct PathLike {
        path: PathBuf,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for PathLike {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field1_finish(
                f,
                "PathLike",
                "path",
                &&self.path,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for PathLike {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> PathLike {
            PathLike {
                path: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.path),
            }
        }
    }
    impl PathLike {
        pub fn new<P: Into<PathBuf>>(path: P) -> Self {
            PathLike { path: path.into() }
        }
        pub fn name(&self) -> Option<String> {
            self.path.file_name().and_then(|s| Some(s.to_string_lossy().into_owned()))
        }
        pub fn stem(&self) -> Option<String> {
            self.path.file_stem().and_then(|s| Some(s.to_string_lossy().into_owned()))
        }
        pub fn extension(&self) -> Option<String> {
            self.path.extension().and_then(|s| Some(s.to_string_lossy().into_owned()))
        }
        pub fn parent(&self) -> Option<&Path> {
            self.path.parent()
        }
        pub fn as_str(&self) -> &str {
            self.path.to_str().unwrap_or("")
        }
        pub fn join<P: AsRef<Path>>(&self, child: P) -> PathLike {
            PathLike {
                path: self.path.join(child),
            }
        }
    }
}
pub use util::*;
mod graph {
    use crate::*;
    use rustworkx_core::petgraph;
    use rustworkx_core::petgraph::{graph::NodeIndex, Directed, Direction, Graph};
    pub struct DiGraph<N, K> {
        pub map: Dict<N, NodeIndex>,
        pub graph: Graph<NodeData<N, K>, (), Directed>,
        edges: Set<(u32, u32)>,
        cache_ancestor: Dict<usize, Vec<(usize, usize)>>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<N: ::core::fmt::Debug, K: ::core::fmt::Debug> ::core::fmt::Debug
    for DiGraph<N, K> {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "DiGraph",
                "map",
                &self.map,
                "graph",
                &self.graph,
                "edges",
                &self.edges,
                "cache_ancestor",
                &&self.cache_ancestor,
            )
        }
    }
    pub struct NodeData<N, K> {
        pub key: N,
        pub data: K,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<N: ::core::fmt::Debug, K: ::core::fmt::Debug> ::core::fmt::Debug
    for NodeData<N, K> {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field2_finish(
                f,
                "NodeData",
                "key",
                &self.key,
                "data",
                &&self.data,
            )
        }
    }
    impl<N: Default + Eq + Hash + Clone, K: Default> DiGraph<N, K> {
        pub fn new() -> Self {
            Self {
                map: Dict::new(),
                graph: Graph::new(),
                edges: Set::new(),
                cache_ancestor: Dict::new(),
            }
        }
        pub fn add_node(&mut self, key: N, data: Option<K>) {
            let nodedata = NodeData {
                key: key.clone(),
                data: data.unwrap_or(Default::default()),
            };
            let node = self.graph.add_node(nodedata);
            self.map.insert(key, node);
        }
        pub fn add_edge(&mut self, a: N, b: N) {
            let node1 = self.map.get(&a).expect("Node not found");
            let node2 = self.map.get(&b).expect("Node not found");
            self.graph.add_edge(*node1, *node2, ());
        }
        pub fn outgoings(&self, a: &N) -> Vec<&N> {
            if !self.map.contains_key(a) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Node not found"));
                }
            }
            self.graph
                .neighbors_directed(*self.map.get(a).unwrap(), Direction::Outgoing)
                .map(|x| &self.graph[x].key)
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn incomings(&self, a: &N) -> Vec<&N> {
            self.graph
                .neighbors_directed(*self.map.get(a).unwrap(), Direction::Incoming)
                .map(|x| &self.graph[x].key)
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn get_node(&mut self, key: N) -> &mut K {
            let ni = self.map.get(&key).unwrap();
            &mut self.graph[*ni].data
        }
        pub fn nodes(&self) -> Vec<&N> {
            self.map.keys().collect()
        }
        pub fn remove_node(&mut self, a: &N) {
            let last_node = NodeIndex::new(self.graph.node_count() - 1);
            let last_node_key = &self.graph[last_node].key;
            let node = *self.map.get(a).unwrap();
            if a != last_node_key {
                *self.map.get_mut(last_node_key).unwrap() = node;
            }
            self.graph.remove_node(node);
            self.map.remove(a);
        }
        pub fn toposort(&self) -> Vec<usize> {
            petgraph::algo::toposort(&self.graph, None)
                .unwrap()
                .into_iter()
                .map(|x| x.index())
                .collect()
        }
    }
    impl<N: Default + Eq + Hash + Clone, K: Default> Index<N> for DiGraph<N, K> {
        type Output = K;
        fn index(&self, index: N) -> &Self::Output {
            let ni = self.map.get(&index).unwrap();
            &self.graph[*ni].data
        }
    }
    impl<N: Default + Eq + Hash + Clone, K: Default> IndexMut<N> for DiGraph<N, K> {
        fn index_mut(&mut self, index: N) -> &mut Self::Output {
            let ni = self.map.get(&index).unwrap();
            &mut self.graph[*ni].data
        }
    }
}
pub use graph::*;
pub mod rtree {
    use crate::*;
    use rstar::{primitives::Rectangle, RTree, AABB};
    pub struct Rtree {
        tree: RTree<Rectangle<[float; 2]>>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for Rtree {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Rtree {
            Rtree {
                tree: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Rtree {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field1_finish(
                f,
                "Rtree",
                "tree",
                &&self.tree,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Rtree {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Rtree {
            Rtree {
                tree: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.tree),
            }
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Display for Rtree {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
            let mut s = String::new();
            for point in self.tree.iter() {
                s.push_str(
                    &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!("[{0:?} {1:?}]\n", point.lower(), point.upper()),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                );
            }
            f.write_fmt(format_args!("{0}", s))
        }
    }
    impl Rtree {
        pub fn new() -> Self {
            Default::default()
        }
        pub fn insert(&mut self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) {
            self.tree.insert(Rectangle::from_corners(a, b));
        }
        pub fn bulk_insert(&mut self, a: Vec<[[float; 2]; 2]>) {
            self.tree = RTree::bulk_load(
                a.iter().map(|x| Rectangle::from_corners(x[0], x[1])).collect(),
            );
        }
        pub fn count(&self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) -> usize {
            self.tree.locate_in_envelope_intersecting(&AABB::from_corners(a, b)).count()
        }
        pub fn intersection(
            &self,
            a: [float; 2],
            b: [float; 2],
        ) -> Vec<[[float; 2]; 2]> {
            self.tree
                .locate_in_envelope_intersecting(&AABB::from_corners(a, b))
                .into_iter()
                .map(|x| [x.lower(), x.upper()])
                .collect::<Vec<_>>()
        }
        pub fn nearest(&self, p1: [float; 2]) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            let r = self.tree.nearest_neighbor(&p1).unwrap();
            [r.lower(), r.upper()]
        }
        pub fn pop_nearest(&mut self, p1: [float; 2]) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            let r = self.tree.pop_nearest_neighbor(&p1).unwrap();
            [r.lower(), r.upper()]
        }
        pub fn nearest_within(
            &self,
            p1: [float; 2],
            mut radius: float,
        ) -> Vec<[[float; 2]; 2]> {
            radius += 1e-2;
            self.tree
                .locate_within_distance(p1, radius * radius * 2.0)
                .into_iter()
                .map(|x| [x.lower(), x.upper()])
                .collect::<Vec<_>>()
        }
        pub fn delete(&mut self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) -> usize {
            self.tree.drain_in_envelope_intersecting(AABB::from_corners(a, b)).count()
        }
        pub fn size(&self) -> usize {
            self.tree.size()
        }
        pub fn __str__(&self) -> String {
            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("{0:?}", self.tree));
                res
            })
        }
    }
}
pub use rtree::*;
pub mod rtree_id {
    use crate::*;
    use rstar::{
        primitives::{GeomWithData, Rectangle},
        RTree, RTreeObject, AABB,
    };
    type Element<T> = GeomWithData<Rectangle<[float; 2]>, T>;
    pub struct RtreeWithData<T> {
        tree: RTree<Element<T>>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<T: ::core::default::Default> ::core::default::Default for RtreeWithData<T> {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> RtreeWithData<T> {
            RtreeWithData {
                tree: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<T: ::core::fmt::Debug> ::core::fmt::Debug for RtreeWithData<T> {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field1_finish(
                f,
                "RtreeWithData",
                "tree",
                &&self.tree,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<T: ::core::clone::Clone> ::core::clone::Clone for RtreeWithData<T> {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> RtreeWithData<T> {
            RtreeWithData {
                tree: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.tree),
            }
        }
    }
    impl<T> fmt::Display for RtreeWithData<T> {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
            let mut s = String::new();
            for point in self.tree.iter() {
                s.push_str(
                    &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "[{0:?} {1:?}]\n",
                                point.geom().lower(),
                                point.geom().upper(),
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                );
            }
            f.write_fmt(format_args!("{0}", s))
        }
    }
    impl<T: Default + Copy> RtreeWithData<T> {
        pub fn new() -> Self {
            Default::default()
        }
        pub fn insert(&mut self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2], data: T) {
            self.tree.insert(GeomWithData::new(Rectangle::from_corners(a, b), data));
        }
        pub fn bulk_insert(&mut self, a: Vec<([[float; 2]; 2], T)>) {
            self.tree = RTree::bulk_load(
                a
                    .iter()
                    .map(|x| GeomWithData::new(
                        Rectangle::from_corners(x.0[0], x.0[1]),
                        x.1,
                    ))
                    .collect(),
            );
        }
        pub fn count(&self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) -> usize {
            self.tree.locate_in_envelope_intersecting(&AABB::from_corners(a, b)).count()
        }
        pub fn intersection(&self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) -> Vec<&Element<T>> {
            self.tree
                .locate_in_envelope_intersecting(&AABB::from_corners(a, b))
                .into_iter()
                .collect::<Vec<_>>()
        }
        pub fn nearest(&self, p1: [float; 2]) -> &Element<T> {
            self.tree.nearest_neighbor(&p1).unwrap()
        }
        pub fn pop_nearest(&mut self, p1: [float; 2]) -> Element<T> {
            self.tree.pop_nearest_neighbor(&p1).unwrap()
        }
        pub fn delete(&mut self, a: [float; 2], b: [float; 2]) -> usize {
            self.tree.drain_in_envelope_intersecting(AABB::from_corners(a, b)).count()
        }
        pub fn size(&self) -> usize {
            self.tree.size()
        }
        pub fn is_empty(&self) -> bool {
            self.tree.size() == 0
        }
    }
}
pub use rtree_id::*;

            mod forbid {
                pub trait Drop {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                #[allow(drop_bounds)]
                impl<T: ?::cxx::core::marker::Sized + ::cxx::core::ops::Drop> self::Drop
                for T {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::Vector2 {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::Tuple2_int {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::Tuple2_float {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::List_int {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::List_float {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::NodeInfo {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::SpatialInfo {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::TileInfo {}
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl self::Drop for super::Pair_Int_ListFloat {}
            }
        };
    }
    impl ffi::Vector2 {
        pub fn new(x: f64, y: f64) -> Self {
            Self { x, y }
        }
    }
    impl ffi::Tuple2_int {
        pub fn new(first: i32, second: i32) -> Self {
            Self { first, second }
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Debug for ffi::Tuple2_int {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
            f.write_fmt(format_args!("({0}, {1})", self.first, self.second))
        }
    }
    impl<T: CCi32> From<(T, T)> for ffi::Tuple2_int {
        fn from(tuple: (T, T)) -> Self {
            Self {
                first: tuple.0.i32(),
                second: tuple.1.i32(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl<T: CCi32> From<Vec<T>> for ffi::List_int {
        fn from(elements: Vec<T>) -> Self {
            Self {
                elements: elements.into_iter().map(|x| x.i32()).collect(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Index<usize> for ffi::List_int {
        type Output = i32;
        fn index(&self, index: usize) -> &Self::Output {
            &self.elements[index]
        }
    }
    impl ffi::List_int {
        pub fn len(&self) -> usize {
            self.elements.len()
        }
        pub fn iter(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &i32> {
            self.elements.iter()
        }
    }
    impl<T: CCf64> From<Vec<T>> for ffi::List_float {
        fn from(elements: Vec<T>) -> Self {
            Self {
                elements: elements.into_iter().map(|x| x.f64()).collect(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Index<usize> for ffi::List_float {
        type Output = f64;
        fn index(&self, index: usize) -> &Self::Output {
            &self.elements[index]
        }
    }
    impl ffi::List_float {
        pub fn len(&self) -> usize {
            self.elements.len()
        }
        pub fn iter(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &f64> {
            self.elements.iter()
        }
    }
    impl ffi::SpatialInfo {
        pub fn positions(&self) -> Vec<(i32, i32)> {
            self.positions.iter().map(|x| (x.first, x.second)).collect()
        }
    }
    impl From<(i32, Vec<f64>)> for ffi::Pair_Int_ListFloat {
        fn from(pair: (i32, Vec<f64>)) -> Self {
            Self {
                first: pair.0,
                second: pair.1.into(),
            }
        }
    }
}

centers = km.cluster_centers_\n    cluster_sizes = np.bincount(labels)\n    if method == 0:\n        for cluster_id in range(max(labels) + 1):\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[np.where(cluster_sizes >= 4)] = np.inf\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 1:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # print(\"--\")\n                # print(cluster_sizes[cluster_id])\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[walked_id] = np.inf\n                # print(walked_id)\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n                # print(new_cluster_id)\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 2:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = scipy.spatial.distance.cdist(points[cluster_points], centers)\n                distances[:, walked_id] = np.inf\n                selected_idx, new_cluster_id = np.unravel_index(\n                    np.argmin(distances), distances.shape\n                )\n                cheapest_point_idx = cluster_points[selected_idx]\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    for i in range(len(km.cluster_centers_)):\n        km.cluster_centers_[i] = np.mean(points[np.where(labels == i)], axis=0)\n\n    return km\n\n\ndef evaluate(points, centers, labels, output=False):\n    km_obj = 0\n    for i, point in enumerate(points):\n        km_obj += np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(centers[labels[i]]))\n    if output:\n        print(\"objective value:\", km_obj)\n    return km_obj\n\n\ndef plot_points_with_centers(points, centers, labels, colors):\n    plt.figure()\n plt.gca().figure.tight_layout()\n    plot_images(plt.gcf(), 500)\n    plt.close()\n\n\ndef solve_tiling_problem(grid_size, tiles, tiles_weight, tile_limits, spatial_occupancy, output):\n    import gurobipy as gp\n    from gurobipy import GRB\n\n    spatial_occupancy = np.asarray(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(\"grid_size:\", grid_size)\n    # print(\"tiles:\", tiles)\n    # print(\"tiles_weight:\", tiles_weight)\n    # print(\"tile_limits:\", tile_limits)\n    # print(\"spatial_occupancy:\", spatial_occupancy)\n    assert spatial_occupancy.shape == grid_size\n    # Define grid and tile sizes\n    N, M = grid_size  # Grid size (width, height)\n    # tiles = [(1, 2), (2, 1), (2, 2)]  # Tile types (width, height)\n    # tile_limits = [20, 25, 2]  # Limits for each tile type (max tiles)\n    # spatial_occupancy = np.transpose(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(spatial_occupancy.shape)\n    tiles_area = [w * h for w, h in tiles]\n    # Create model\n    model = gp.Model(\"RectangularTiling\")\n    if not output:\n        model.Params.OutputFlag = 0\n    model.Params.Threads = min(24, os.cpu_count())\n    # Decision variables\n    x = model.addVars(len(tiles), N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"x\")  # Tile placement\n    y = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"y\")  # Cell coverage\n    y_weight = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS)\n\n    # Spatial occupancy constraints\n    # if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n    #     for i in range(N):\n    #         for j in range(M):\n    #             if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n    #                 for k in range(len(tiles)):\n    #                     model.addConstr(x[k, i, j] == 0)\n\n    # Tile placement constraints\n    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s within the bounds of any tile placement\n            model.addConstr(\n                y[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                )\n                + spatial_occupancy[i][j],\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n            model.addConstr(\n                y_weight[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c] / tiles_area[k] * tiles_weight[k]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                ),\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n\n    # Non-overlapping constraints: Each cell can be covered by at most one tile\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            model.addConstr(y[i, j] <= 1, name=f\"no_overlap_{i}_{j}\")\n\n    # Tile count limits\n    if len(tile_limits) > 0:\n        for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n  P.show(save=True)\n\n\ndef kmean_alg(method, points, N):\n    K = len(points) // N + 1  # Number of clusters\n    plt.figure()\n    km = KMeans(n_clusters=K).fit(points)\n    labels = km.labels_\n    centers = km.cluster_centers_\n    cluster_sizes = np.bincount(labels)\n    if method == 0:\n        for cluster_id in range(max(labels) + 1):\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[np.where(cluster_sizes >= 4)] = np.inf\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 1:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # print(\"--\")\n                # print(cluster_sizes[cluster_id])\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[walked_id] = np.inf\n                # print(walked_id)\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n                # print(new_cluster_id)\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 2:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = scipy.spatial.distance.cdist(points[cluster_points], centers)\n                distances[:, walked_id] = np.inf\n                selected_idx, new_cluster_id = np.unravel_index(\n                    np.argmin(distances), distances.shape\n                )\n                cheapest_point_idx = cluster_points[selected_idx]\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    for i in range(len(km.cluster_centers_)):\n        km.cluster_centers_[i] = np.mean(points[np.where(labels == i)], axis=0)\n\n    return km\n\n\ndef evaluate(points, centers, labels, output=False):\n    km_obj = 0\n    for i, point in enumerate(points):\n        km_obj += np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(centers[labels[i]]))\n    if output:\n        print(\"objective value:\", km_obj)\n    return km_obj\n\n\ndef plot_points_with_centers(points, centers, labels, colors):\n    plt.figure()\n lp_plot(points, N, method, labels):\n    M = np.abs(points).sum()\n    num_points = len(points)\n    K = num_points // N + 1  # Number of clusters\n    # colors = np.random.rand(K, 3)\n    index =       # model.Params.TimeLimit = 60\n            model.Params.WorkLimit = 120\n            model.Params.Threads = min(24, os.cpu_count())\n            # model.Params.ScaleFlag = 1\n            #           group_centroid_gap_abs = model.addVars(\n                index, cindex, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS, lb=-GRB.INFINITY\n            )\n            # min_val = model.addVars(cindex,                   label = labels[i]\n                    x[i, label].start = 1\n\n            for i in index:\n                model.addConstr(quicksum(x[i, j] for j in cindex) == 1)\n            for                          (group_centroid_gap[i, j, 1] == (group_centroid[j, 1] - points[i][1]))\n                        )\n\n                        model.addConstr(\n             * x[i, j]\n                        )\n\n                model.setObjective(\n                    quicksum(\n                        quicksum((group_centroid_gap_abs[i, j]) for i in index) current_obj = model.cbGet(GRB.Callback.MIPSOL_OBJ)\n                    print(\"--------------------\")\n                    print(current_obj)\n                    # Check if it\'s the first solution gurobipy as gp\n    from gurobipy import GRB\n\n    spatial_occupancy = np.asarray(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(\"grid_size:\", grid_size)\n    # print(\"tiles:\", tiles)\n    # print(\"tiles_weight:\", tiles_weight)\n    # print(\"tile_limits:\", tile_limits)\n    # print(\"spatial_occupancy:\", spatial_occupancy)\n    assert spatial_occupancy.shape == grid_size\n    # Define grid and tile sizes\n    N, M = grid_size  # Grid size (width, height)\n    # tiles = [(1, 2), (2, 1), (2, 2)]  # Tile types (width, height)\n    # tile_limits = [20, 25, 2]  # Limits for each tile type (max tiles)\n    # spatial_occupancy = np.transpose(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(spatial_occupancy.shape)\n    tiles_area = [w * h for w, h in tiles]\n    # Create model\n    model = gp.Model(\"RectangularTiling\")\n    if not output:\n        model.Params.OutputFlag = 0\n    model.Params.Threads = min(24, os.cpu_count())\n    # Decision variables\n    x = model.addVars(len(tiles), N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"x\")  # Tile placement\n    y = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"y\")  # Cell coverage\n    y_weight = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS)\n\n    # Spatial occupancy constraints\n    # if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n    #     for i in range(N):\n    #         for j in range(M):\n    #             if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n    #                 for k in range(len(tiles)):\n    #                     model.addConstr(x[k, i, j] == 0)\n\n    # Tile placement constraints\n    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s within the bounds of any tile placement\n            model.addConstr(\n                y[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                )\n                + spatial_occupancy[i][j],\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n            model.addConstr(\n                y_weight[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c] / tiles_area[k] * tiles_weight[k]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                ),\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n\n    # Non-overlapping constraints: Each cell can be covered by at most one tile\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            model.addConstr(y[i, j] <= 1, name=f\"no_overlap_{i}_{j}\")\n\n    # Tile count limits\n    if len(tile_limits) > 0:\n        for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n            model.addConstr(\n                gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)) <= tile_limits[k],\n                name=f\"tile_limit_{k}\",\n            )\n\n    # Objective: Maximize total coverage\n    # model.setObjective(gp.quicksum(y[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE)\n    model.setObjective(\n        gp.quicksum(y_weight[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE\n    )\n\n    # Solve the model\n    model.optimize()\n    # Print solution\n    if model.status == GRB.OPTIMAL:\n        # print(\"Optimal solution found!\")\n        # for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        #     print(f\"Tile type {k} ({tile_h}x{tile_w}):\")\n        #     for i in range(N):\n        #         for j in range(M):\n        #             if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n        #                 print(f\"  Placed at ({i}, {j})\")\n\n        capcaity = np.zeros(len(tiles), dtype=int)\n        for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n            for i in range(N):\n                for j in range(M):\n                    if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                        capcaity[k] += 1\n        if output:\n            # draw layout using matplotlib\n            layout = np.zeros((N, M))\n            for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                            layout[i : i + tile_h, j : j + tile_w] = k + 1\n\n            if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n                            for k in range(len(tiles)):\n                                layout[i, j] = len(tiles) + 1\n            plot_binary_image(layout, aspect_ratio=1, title=\"Tile placements\", grid=True)\n            # layout = np.zeros((N, M))\n            # for i in range(N):\n            #     for j in     impl Pyo3Cell {
        pub fn new(inst: &SharedInst) -> Self {
            let name = inst.borrow().name.clone();
            let x = inst.borrow().x;
            let y = inst.borrow().y;
            let width = inst.borrow().width();
            let height = inst.borrow().height();
            let walked = inst.borrow().walked;
            let highlighted = inst.borrow().highlighted;
            let pins = Vec::new();
            Self {
                name,
                x,
                y,
                width,
                height,
                walked,
                highlighted,
                pins,
            }
        }
    }

        __radius: ::typed_builder::Optional<int>,
    > PyExtraVisualBuilder<
        ((String,), (Vec<(float, float)>,), __line_width, __color, __angle, __radius),
    > {
        #[allow(
            clippy::default_trait_access,
            clippy::used_underscore_binding,
            clippy::no_effect_underscore_binding
        )]
        pub fn build(self) -> PyExtraVisual {
            let (id, points, line_width, color, angle, radius) = self.fields;
            let id = id.0;
            let points = points.0;
            let line_width = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(line_width, || 1);
            let color = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(color, || (0, 0, 0));
            let angle = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(angle, || 0);
            let radius = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(radius, || 3);
            #[allow(deprecated)]
            PyExtraVisual {
                id,
                points,
                line_width,
                color,
                angle,
                radius,
            }
                .into()
        }
    }

pub use bridge_py::*;
pub mod numpy {
    use crate::util;
    use crate::{Deserialize, Serialize};
    use castaway::cast as cast_special;
    use ndarray::prelude::*;
    use ndarray::{ArrayBase, Data, Dimension};
    use num::cast::NumCast;
    use num_cast::*;
    use num_cast::*;
    use ordered_float::{FloatCore, OrderedFloat};
    use std::ops::{Index, IndexMut, Range};
    pub fn unravel_index(index: usize, shape: &[usize]) -> Vec<usize> {
        if !(index < shape.iter().product::<usize>()) {
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!(
                        "ValueError: index {0} is out of bounds for array with size {1}",
                        index,
                        shape.iter().product::<usize>(),
                    ),
                );
            }
        }
        let mut result = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(0, shape.len());
        let mut remainder = index;
        for (i, &dim) in shape.iter().rev().enumerate() {
            result[shape.len() - 1 - i] = remainder % dim;
            remainder /= dim;
        }
        result
    }
    pub fn bincount(values: &[usize]) -> Vec<usize> {
        let max_value = values.iter().max().unwrap();
        let mut result = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(0, max_value + 1);
        for &value in values {
            result[value] += 1;
        }
        result
    }
    pub fn index<T: Copy, F>(labels: &[T], condition: F) -> Vec<usize>
    where
        F: Fn(T) -> bool,
    {
        labels
            .iter()
            .enumerate()
            .filter_map(|(index, &value)| {
                if condition(value) { Some(index) } else { None }
            })
            .collect()
    }
    fn take_row<'a>(a: &'a Array2<f64>, indices: &[usize]) -> Vec<ArrayView1<'a, f64>> {
        indices.iter().map(|&i| a.row(i)).collect()
    }
    fn take_column<'a>(
        a: &'a Array2<f64>,
        indices: &[usize],
    ) -> Vec<ArrayView1<'a, f64>> {
        indices.iter().map(|&i| a.column(i)).collect()
    }
    pub fn take<'a>(
        a: &'a Array2<f64>,
        indices: &[usize],
        axis: usize,
    ) -> Vec<ArrayView1<'a, f64>> {
        match axis {
            0 => take_row(a, indices),
            1 => take_column(a, indices),
            _ => {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Axis must be 0 or 1"));
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn take_clone<'a>(
        a: &'a Array2<f64>,
        indices: &[usize],
        axis: usize,
    ) -> Array2<f64> {
        match axis {
            0 => a.select(Axis(0), indices),
            1 => a.select(Axis(1), indices),
            _ => {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Axis must be 0 or 1"));
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn argmin<S, D, T>(array: &ArrayBase<S, D>) -> usize
    where
        S: Data<Elem = T>,
        D: Dimension,
        T: PartialOrd + Copy + FloatCore,
    {
        array
            .iter()
            .enumerate()
            .min_by_key(|&(_, &value)| OrderedFloat(value))
            .map(|(idx, _)| idx)
            .unwrap()
    }
    pub fn mean_array(
        array: &Array<f64, ndarray::Dim<[usize; 2]>>,
        axis: usize,
    ) -> Array<f64, ndarray::Dim<[usize; 1]>> {
        let axis = Axis(axis);
        array
            .mean_axis(axis)
            .expect("Mean calculation failed. Check array shape and axis.")
    }
    pub fn row_mean<'a>(
        array: &'a Vec<ArrayView1<'a, f64>>,
    ) -> Array<f64, ndarray::Dim<[usize; 1]>> {
        if array.is_empty() {
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!("Input array vector is empty."),
                );
            };
        }
        for arr in array {
            if !(arr.len() == array[0].len()) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("All arrays must have the same length."),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        let mut sum_array = Array::zeros(array[0].len());
        for arr in array {
            sum_array = &sum_array + arr;
        }
        let count = array.len() as f64;
        sum_array / count
    }
    pub fn array2d<T: Clone>(double_vec: Vec<Vec<T>>) -> Result<Array2<T>, String> {
        if double_vec.is_empty() || double_vec[0].is_empty() {
            return Err("Input Vec<Vec<T>> is empty or contains empty rows".to_string());
        }
        let rows = double_vec.len();
        let cols = double_vec[0].len();
        if !double_vec.iter().all(|row| row.len() == cols) {
            return Err("Input Vec<Vec<T>> rows have inconsistent lengths".to_string());
        }
        let flat_vec: Vec<T> = double_vec.into_iter().flatten().collect();
        Array2::from_shape_vec((rows, cols), flat_vec).map_err(|e| e.to_string())
    }
    pub struct Array2D<T> {
        pub data: Vec<T>,
        _shape: (usize, usize),
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<T: ::core::fmt::Debug> ::core::fmt::Debug for Array2D<T> {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field2_finish(
                f,
                "Array2D",
                "data",
                &self.data,
                "_shape",
                &&self._shape,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<T: ::core::default::Default> ::core::default::Default for Array2D<T> {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Array2D<T> {
            Array2D {
                data: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                _shape: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }

                        _serde::__private::Formatter::write_str(

                        self,
