    impl<T> Array2D<T> {
        pub fn new<K>(data: Vec<T>, shape: (K, K)) -> Self
        where
            K: num_cast::CCusize,
        {
            let shape = (shape.0.usize(), shape.1.usize());
            if !(data.len() == shape.0 * shape.1) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Data length does not match shape"),
                    );
                }
            }
            Self { data, _shape: shape }
        }
        pub fn shape(&self) -> (usize, usize) {
            self._shape
        }
        pub fn size(&self) -> usize {
            self.data.len()
        }
        pub fn view(&self) -> Array2D<&T> {
            Array2D {
                data: self.data.iter().collect(),
                _shape: self._shape,
            }
        }
    }
    impl<T> Index<(usize, usize)> for Array2D<T> {
        type Output = T;
        fn index(&self, index: (usize, usize)) -> &T {
            let (row, col) = index;
            if !(row < self._shape.0) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Row index out of bounds"),
                    );
                }
            }
            if !(col < self._shape.1) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Column index out of bounds"),
                    );
                }
            }
            &self.data[row * self._shape.1 + col]
        }
    }
    impl<T> Array2D<T> {
        pub fn iter(&self) -> std::slice::Iter<T> {
            self.data.iter()
        }
        pub fn iter_mut(&mut self) -> std::slice::IterMut<T> {
            self.data.iter_mut()
        }
        pub fn into_iter(self) -> std::vec::IntoIter<T> {
            self.data.into_iter()
        }
        pub fn slice<K: 'static>(&self, ranges: K) -> Array2D<&T> {
            let (rows, cols) = self._shape;
            if let Ok(range) = {
                #[allow(unused_imports)]
                use ::castaway::internal::*;
                let value = &ranges;
                let src_token = CastToken::of_val(&value);
                let dest_token = CastToken::<&Range<usize>>::of();
                let result: ::core::result::Result<&Range<usize>, _> = (&&&&&&&(
                    src_token,
                    dest_token,
                ))
                    .try_cast(value);
                result
            } {
                if !(range.start < rows && range.end <= rows) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!("Row range out of bounds"),
                        );
                    }
                }
                let data = self
                    .data[(range.start * cols)..(range.end * cols)]
                    .iter()
                    .collect();
                return Array2D {
                    data: data,
                    _shape: (range.end - range.start, cols),
                };
            } else if let Ok(range) = {
                #[allow(unused_imports)]
                use ::castaway::internal::*;
                let value = &ranges;
                let src_token = CastToken::of_val(&value);
                let dest_token = CastToken::<&Range<i32>>::of();
                let result: ::core::result::Result<&Range<i32>, _> = (&&&&&&&(
                    src_token,
                    dest_token,
                ))
                    .try_cast(value);
                result
            } {
                let range_usize = (range.start.usize())..(range.end.usize());
                return self.slice(range_usize);
            } else if let Ok(ranges) = {
                #[allow(unused_imports)]
                use ::castaway::internal::*;
                let value = &ranges;
                let src_token = CastToken::of_val(&value);
                let dest_token = CastToken::<&(Range<usize>, Range<usize>)>::of();
                let result: ::core::result::Result<&(Range<usize>, Range<usize>), _> = (&&&&&&&(
                    src_token,
                    dest_token,
                ))
                    .try_cast(value);
                result
            } {
                if !(ranges.0.start < rows && ranges.0.end <= rows) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!("Row range out of bounds"),
                        );
                    }
                }
                if !(ranges.1.start < cols && ranges.1.end <= cols) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!("Column range out of bounds"),
                        );
                    }
                }
                let mut data = Vec::with_capacity(
                    (ranges.0.end - ranges.0.start) * (ranges.1.end - ranges.1.start),
                );
                for i in ranges.0.start..ranges.0.end {
                    let start = i * cols + ranges.1.start;
                    let end = i * cols + ranges.1.end;
                    for j in start..end {
                        data.push(&self.data[j]);
                    }
                }
                return Array2D {
                    data: data,
                    _shape: (
                        ranges.0.end - ranges.0.start,
                        ranges.1.end - ranges.1.start,
                    ),
                };
            } else if let Ok(ranges) = {
                #[allow(unused_imports)]
                use ::castaway::internal::*;
                let value = &ranges;
                let src_token = CastToken::of_val(&value);
                let dest_token = CastToken::<&(Range<i32>, Range<i32>)>::of();
                let result: ::core::result::Result<&(Range<i32>, Range<i32>), _> = (&&&&&&&(
                    src_token,
                    dest_token,
                ))
                    .try_cast(value);
                result
            } {
                let range0_usize = (ranges.0.start.usize())..(ranges.0.end.usize());
                let range1_usize = (ranges.1.start.usize())..(ranges.1.end.usize());
                return self.slice((range0_usize, range1_usize));
            }
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Invalid range type"));
            };
        }
        pub fn last(&self) -> &T {
            self.data.last().unwrap()
        }
    }
    fn linspace_float(start: f64, end: f64, num: usize) -> Vec<f64> {
        if num == 1 {
            return <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([start]));
        }
        let step = (end - start) / (num - 1).f64();
        (0..num).map(|i| start + i.f64() * step).collect()
    }
    fn linspace_int(start: i64, end: i64, num: usize) -> Vec<i64> {
        if num == 1 {
            return <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([start]));
        }
        let chunk_size = util::int_ceil_div(end - start, (num - 1).i64()).usize();
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        result.extend((start..end).step_by(chunk_size));
        result.push(end);
        result
    }
    pub fn linspace<T: TypeCheck>(start: T, end: T, num: usize) -> Vec<T>
    where
        T: NumCast + num::Num,
    {
        if !(num > 0) {
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!("Number of samples must be non-negative"),
                );
            }
        }
        if start.is_float() {
            return linspace_float(
                    NumCast::from(start).unwrap(),
                    NumCast::from(end).unwrap(),
                    num,
                )
                .iter()
                .map(|&x| NumCast::from(x).unwrap())
                .collect();
        } else if start.is_integer() {
            let result = linspace_float(
                    NumCast::from(start).unwrap(),
                    NumCast::from(end).unwrap(),
                    num,
                )
                .into_iter()
                .map(|x| NumCast::from(x).unwrap())
                .collect();
            return result;
        }
        {
            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Invalid range type"));
        };
    }
}
pub mod scipy {
    use ndarray::prelude::*;
    use ordered_float::OrderedFloat;
    pub fn cdist_array(a: &Array2<f64>, b: &Array2<f64>) -> Array2<f64> {
        let (m, _) = a.dim();
        let (n, _) = b.dim();
        let mut result = Array2::<f64>::zeros((m, n));
        for i in 0..m {
            for j in 0..n {
                let diff = &a.row(i) - &b.row(j);
                result[[i, j]] = diff.dot(&diff).sqrt();
            }
        }
        result
    }
    pub fn cdist_view(a: &Vec<ArrayView1<f64>>, b: &Array2<f64>) -> Array2<f64> {
        let m = a.len();
        let (n, _) = b.dim();
        let mut result = Array2::<f64>::zeros((m, n));
        for i in 0..m {
            for j in 0..n {
                let diff = &a[i] - &b.row(j);
                result[[i, j]] = diff.dot(&diff).sqrt();
            }
        }
        result
    }
    pub(crate) use cdist;
    pub mod cluster {
        use crate::*;
        use kmeans::*;
        fn evaluate_kmeans_quality(
            points: &Array2<float>,
            centers: &Array2<float>,
            labels: &Vec<usize>,
        ) -> float {
            let mut km_obj = 0.0;
            for (i, point) in points.outer_iter().enumerate() {
                let center = centers.row(labels[i]);
                km_obj += norm1((point[0], point[1]), (center[0], center[1]));
            }
            km_obj
        }
        fn reassign_clusters(
            points: &Array2<float>,
            centers: &mut Array2<float>,
            labels: &mut Vec<usize>,
            n_clusters: usize,
            cap: usize,
        ) {
            let mut walked_ids: Set<usize> = Set::new();
            loop {
                let mut cluster_sizes = numpy::bincount(&labels);
                let cluster_id = cluster_sizes.iter().position(|&x| x > cap);
                if cluster_id.is_none() {
                    break;
                }
                let cluster_id = cluster_id.unwrap();
                walked_ids.insert(cluster_id);
                while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > cap {
                    let cluster_indices = numpy::index(labels, |x| x == cluster_id);
                    let filtered_points = numpy::take(&points, &cluster_indices, 0);
                    let mut distances = scipy::cdist_view(&filtered_points, &centers);
                    for walk in walked_ids.iter() {
                        distances.column_mut(*walk).fill(f64::INFINITY);
                    }
                    let min_idx = numpy::unravel_index(
                        numpy::argmin(&distances),
                        distances.shape(),
                    );
                    let (selected_idx, new_cluster_id) = (min_idx[0], min_idx[1]);
                    let cheapest_point_idx = cluster_indices[selected_idx];
                    labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id;
                    cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1;
                    cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1;
                }
                for i in 0..n_clusters {
                    let cluster_indices = numpy::index(labels, |x| x == i);
                    let filtered_points = numpy::take(&points, &cluster_indices, 0);
                    if filtered_points.len() == 0 {
                        continue;
                    }
                    let mean = numpy::row_mean(&filtered_points);
                    centers.row_mut(i).assign(&mean);
                }
            }
            let label_count = numpy::bincount(&labels);
            let mut labels_below_four = (0..label_count.len())
                .filter(|&x| label_count[x] < cap)
                .collect::<Vec<_>>();
            let total_label_count = labels_below_four
                .iter()
                .map(|&x| label_count[x])
                .sum::<usize>();
            if total_label_count >= cap {
                let mut filtered_label_positions = Vec::new();
                for i in 0..labels.len() {
                    for j in 0..labels_below_four.len() {
                        if labels[i] == labels_below_four[j] {
                            filtered_label_positions.push(i);
                        }
                    }
                }
                let points = numpy::take_clone(&points, &filtered_label_positions, 0);
                let mut centers = numpy::take_clone(&centers, &labels_below_four, 0);
                let labels_mapper = labels_below_four
                    .iter()
                    .enumerate()
                    .map(|(i, &x)| (x, i))
                    .collect::<Dict<_, _>>();
                let labels_inv_mapper = labels_below_four
                    .iter()
                    .enumerate()
                    .map(|(i, &x)| (i, x))
                    .collect::<Dict<_, _>>();
                let mut new_labels = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(
                    labels_below_four.len() - 1,
                    filtered_label_positions.len(),
                );
                let n_clusters = labels.len();
                reassign_clusters(
                    &points,
                    &mut centers,
                    &mut new_labels,
                    labels_below_four.len(),
                    cap,
                );
                for i in 0..new_labels.len() {
                    labels[filtered_label_positions[i]] = labels_inv_mapper[&new_labels[i]];
                }
            }
        }
        fn reassign_clusters2(
            points: &Array2<float>,
            centers: &mut Array2<float>,
            labels: &mut Vec<usize>,
            n_clusters: usize,
            cap: usize,
        ) {
            let mut indices = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(Vec::new(), n_clusters);
            for i in 0..labels.len() {
                indices[labels[i]].push(i);
            }
            let mut pq = PriorityQueue::with_default_hasher();
            for i in 0..indices.len() {
                pq.push(i, indices[i].len());
            }
            let mut rtree = RtreeWithData::new();
            for (i, center) in centers.outer_iter().enumerate() {
                let (x, y) = (center[0], center[1]);
                rtree.insert([x, y], [x + 1.0, y + 1.0], i);
            }
            while !pq.is_empty() {
                let front_of_queue = pq.pop().unwrap();
                let cluster_id = front_of_queue.0;
                let mut cluster_size = front_of_queue.1;
                if cluster_size < cap {
                    break;
                }
                let center = centers.row(cluster_id);
                let r = rtree.pop_nearest([center[0], center[1]]);
                {
                    {
                        match (&(r.data), &(cluster_id)) {
                            (left_val, right_val) => {
                                if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                    use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                    {
                                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                            format_args!(
                                                "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                                "",
                                                format_args!(""),
                                                (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                            ),
                                        );
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    };
                };
                let mut changed_ids = Set::new();
                while cluster_size > cap {
                    let cluster_indices = &indices[cluster_id];
                    let filtered_points = numpy::take(
                        &points,
                        cluster_indices.as_slice(),
                        0,
                    );
                    let mut buffer = Vec::new();
                    for point in filtered_points {
                        let closest_center = rtree.nearest([point[0], point[1]]);
                        let center_pos = closest_center.geom().lower();
                        let center_id = closest_center.data;
                        let dis_to_center = norm2(
                            point[0],
                            point[1],
                            center_pos[0],
                            center_pos[1],
                        );
                        buffer.push((dis_to_center, center_id));
                    }
                    let min_idx = numeric::argmin(&buffer, |x| x.0);
                    let new_cluster_id = buffer[min_idx].1;
                    let cheapest_point_idx = cluster_indices[min_idx];
                    labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id;
                    if let Some(pos) = indices[cluster_id]
                        .iter()
                        .position(|&x| x == cheapest_point_idx)
                    {
                        indices[cluster_id].swap_remove(pos);
                    }
                    indices[new_cluster_id].push(cheapest_point_idx);
                    pq.change_priority_by(&cluster_id, |x| *x -= 1);
                    pq.change_priority_by(&new_cluster_id, |x| *x += 1);
                    changed_ids.insert(new_cluster_id);
                    cluster_size -= 1;
                }
                centers
                    .row_mut(cluster_id)
                    .assign(
                        &numpy::row_mean(&numpy::take(&points, &indices[cluster_id], 0)),
                    );
                for id in changed_ids {
                    let cluster_indices = &indices[id];
                    let filtered_points = numpy::take(&points, cluster_indices, 0);
                    let mean = numpy::row_mean(&filtered_points);
                    let ori_center = centers.row(id).iter().cloned().collect_vec();
                    centers.row_mut(id).assign(&mean);
                    let r = rtree.pop_nearest([ori_center[0], ori_center[1]]);
                    {
                        {
                            match (&(r.data), &(id)) {
                                (left_val, right_val) => {
                                    if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                        use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                        {
                                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                                format_args!(
                                                    "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                                    "",
                                                    format_args!(""),
                                                    (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                                ),
                                            );
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        };
                    };
                    rtree.insert([mean[0], mean[1]], [mean[0] + 1.0, mean[1] + 1.0], id);
                }
            }
            let mut labels_below_cap = indices
                .into_iter()
                .filter(|x| x.len() < cap)
                .flatten()
                .collect_vec();
            labels_below_cap
                .chunks(cap)
                .for_each(|x| {
                    if x.len() == cap {
                        let first_label = labels[x[0]];
                        x.iter()
                            .for_each(|&x| {
                                labels[x] = first_label;
                            });
                        centers
                            .row_mut(first_label)
                            .assign(&numpy::row_mean(&numpy::take(&points, x, 0)));
                    }
                });
        }
        pub struct KMeansResult {
            pub samples: Array2<f64>,
            pub cluster_centers: Array2<f64>,
            pub labels: Vec<usize>,
        }
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl ::core::fmt::Debug for KMeansResult {
            #[inline]
            fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
                ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field3_finish(
                    f,
                    "KMeansResult",
                    "samples",
                    &self.samples,
                    "cluster_centers",
                    &self.cluster_centers,
                    "labels",
                    &&self.labels,
                )
            }
        }
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl ::core::default::Default for KMeansResult {
            #[inline]
            fn default() -> KMeansResult {
                KMeansResult {
                    samples: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                    cluster_centers: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                    labels: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                }
            }
        }
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl ::core::clone::Clone for KMeansResult {
            #[inline]
            fn clone(&self) -> KMeansResult {
                KMeansResult {
                    samples: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.samples),
                    cluster_centers: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.cluster_centers),
                    labels: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.labels),
                }
            }
        }
        use bon::builder;
        #[allow(unexpected_cfgs)]
        const _: () = {};
        #[doc(hidden)]
        #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments, clippy::fn_params_excessive_bools)]
        fn __orig_kmeans(
            samples: Array2<f64>,
            n_clusters: usize,
            cap: Option<usize>,
            n_init: Option<usize>,
            max_iter: Option<usize>,
        ) -> KMeansResult {
            let n_features = 2;
            let num_rows = samples.len_of(Axis(0));
            let model: KMeans<f64, 8, _> = KMeans::new(
                &samples.clone().into_raw_vec_and_offset().0,
                num_rows,
                n_features,
                EuclideanDistance,
            );
            let mut centers = Array2::zeros((n_clusters, n_features));
            let mut labels = Vec::new();
            let mut best_result = float::INFINITY;
            let max_iter = max_iter.unwrap_or(300);
            let n_init = n_init.unwrap_or(10);
            let config = KMeansConfig::build().build();
            for _ in 0..n_init {
                let current_result = model
                    .kmeans_lloyd(
                        n_clusters,
                        max_iter,
                        KMeans::init_random_sample,
                        &config,
                    );
                let current_centers = current_result.centroids.to_vec();
                let mut current_centers = Array2::from_shape_vec(
                        (current_centers.len() / n_features, n_features),
                        current_centers,
                    )
                    .unwrap();
                let mut current_labels = current_result.assignments.clone();
                if let Some(cap) = cap {
                    if !(cap > 0) {
                        {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                format_args!("ValueError: cap must be greater than 0"),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                    if !(cap * n_clusters >= num_rows) {
                        {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                format_args!(
                                    "ValueError: cap * n_clusters must be greater than the number of samples",
                                ),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                    reassign_clusters2(
                        &samples,
                        &mut current_centers,
                        &mut current_labels,
                        n_clusters,
                        cap,
                    );
                }
                let evaluation_result = evaluate_kmeans_quality(
                    &samples,
                    &current_centers,
                    &current_labels,
                );
                if evaluation_result < best_result {
                    best_result = evaluation_result;
                    centers = current_centers;
                    labels = current_labels;
                }
            }
            KMeansResult {
                samples: samples,
                cluster_centers: centers,
                labels,
            }
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        #[allow(clippy::inline_always, clippy::use_self, clippy::missing_const_for_fn)]

                __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                __unsafe_private_named: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }

        impl<S: kmeans_builder::State> KmeansBuilder<S> {
            /// Finishes building and performs the requested action.
            #[inline(always)]

                clippy::inline_always,
                clippy::future_not_send,
                clippy::missing_const_for_fn,

            where
                S: kmeans_builder::IsComplete,
            {
                let samples: Array2<f64> = unsafe {
                    ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(
                        self.__unsafe_private_named.0,
                    )
                };
                let n_clusters: usize = unsafe {
                    ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(
                        self.__unsafe_private_named.1,
                    )
                };
                let cap: Option<usize> = self.__unsafe_private_named.2;
                let n_init: Option<usize> = self.__unsafe_private_named.3;
                let max_iter: Option<usize> = self.__unsafe_private_named.4;
                __orig_kmeans(samples, n_clusters, cap, n_init, max_iter)
            }

*/

            /// Number of initializations to perform
            #[allow(
                clippy::inline_always,
                clippy::impl_trait_in_params,

                }
            }
            /**_**Optional** ([Some](Self::max_iter()) / [Option](Self::maybe_max_iter()) setters)._

*/
            /// Maximum number of iterations for each initialization
            #[allow(
                clippy::inline_always,
                clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
                clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
            )]
            #[inline(always)]
            pub fn max_iter(
                self,
                value: usize,
            ) -> KmeansBuilder<kmeans_builder::SetMaxIter<S>>
            where
                S::MaxIter: kmeans_builder::IsUnset,
            {
                self.maybe_max_iter(Some(value))
            }
            /**_**Optional** ([Some](Self::max_iter()) / [Option](Self::maybe_max_iter()) setters)._

*/
            /// Maximum number of iterations for each initialization
            #[allow(
                clippy::inline_always,
                clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
                clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
            )]
            #[inline(always)]
            pub fn maybe_max_iter(
                mut self,
                value: Option<usize>,
            ) -> KmeansBuilder<kmeans_builder::SetMaxIter<S>>
            where
                S::MaxIter: kmeans_builder::IsUnset,
            {
                self.__unsafe_private_named.4 = value;
                KmeansBuilder {
                    __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                    __unsafe_private_named: self.__unsafe_private_named,
                }
            }
        }
        #[allow(unnameable_types, unreachable_pub, clippy::redundant_pub_crate)]
        /**Tools for manipulating the type state of [`KmeansBuilder`].

See the [detailed guide](https://bon-rs.com/guide/typestate-api) that describes how all the pieces here fit together.*/
        #[allow(deprecated)]
        mod kmeans_builder {
            #[doc(inline)]
            pub use ::bon::__::{IsSet, IsUnset};
            use ::bon::__::{Set, Unset};
            mod sealed {
                pub struct Sealed;
            }
            /**Builder's type state specifies if members are set or not (unset).

You can use the associated types of this trait to control the state of individual members with the [`IsSet`] and [`IsUnset`] traits. You can change the state of the members with the `Set*` structs available in this module.*/
            pub trait State: ::core::marker::Sized {
                /**Type state of the member `samples`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
                type Samples;
                /**Type state of the member `n_clusters`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
                type NClusters;
                /**Type state of the member `cap`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
                type Cap;
                /**Type state of the member `n_init`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
                type NInit;
                /**Type state of the member `max_iter`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
                type MaxIter;
                #[doc(hidden)]
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed;
            }
            /**Marker trait that indicates that all required members are set.

In this state, you can finish building by calling the method [`KmeansBuilder::call()`](super::KmeansBuilder::call())*/
            pub trait IsComplete: State {
                #[doc(hidden)]
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> IsComplete for S
            where
                S::Samples: IsSet,
                S::NClusters: IsSet,
            {
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[deprecated = "this should not be used directly; it is an implementation detail; use the Set* type aliases to control the state of members instead"]
            #[doc(hidden)]
            #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
            mod members {
                pub struct samples(());
                pub struct n_clusters(());
                pub struct cap(());
                pub struct n_init(());
                pub struct max_iter(());
            }
            /// Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsUnset`] implemented for all members.
            ///
            /// This is the initial state of the builder before any setters are called.
            pub struct Empty(());
            /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::Samples`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
            pub struct SetSamples<S: State = Empty>(
                ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
            );
            /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::NClusters`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
            pub struct SetNClusters<S: State = Empty>(
                ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
            );
            /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::Cap`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
            pub struct SetCap<S: State = Empty>(::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>);
            /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::NInit`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
            pub struct SetNInit<S: State = Empty>(
                ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
            );
            /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::MaxIter`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
            pub struct SetMaxIter<S: State = Empty>(
                ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
            );
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl State for Empty {
                type Samples = Unset<members::samples>;
                type NClusters = Unset<members::n_clusters>;
                type Cap = Unset<members::cap>;
                type NInit = Unset<members::n_init>;
                type MaxIter = Unset<members::max_iter>;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> State for SetSamples<S> {
                type Samples = Set<members::samples>;
                type NClusters = S::NClusters;
                type Cap = S::Cap;
                type NInit = S::NInit;
                type MaxIter = S::MaxIter;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> State for SetNClusters<S> {
                type Samples = S::Samples;
                type NClusters = Set<members::n_clusters>;
                type Cap = S::Cap;
                type NInit = S::NInit;
                type MaxIter = S::MaxIter;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> State for SetCap<S> {
                type Samples = S::Samples;
                type NClusters = S::NClusters;
                type Cap = Set<members::cap>;
                type NInit = S::NInit;
                type MaxIter = S::MaxIter;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> State for SetNInit<S> {
                type Samples = S::Samples;
                type NClusters = S::NClusters;
                type Cap = S::Cap;
                type NInit = Set<members::n_init>;
                type MaxIter = S::MaxIter;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
            #[doc(hidden)]
            impl<S: State> State for SetMaxIter<S> {
                type Samples = S::Samples;
                type NClusters = S::NClusters;
                type Cap = S::Cap;
                type NInit = S::NInit;
                type MaxIter = Set<members::max_iter>;
                const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
            }
        }
    }
    pub fn upper_bound(data: &Vec<f64>) -> Option<f64> {
        fn percentile(sorted_data: &Vec<f64>, percentile: f64) -> f64 {
            let index = (percentile / 100.0) * (sorted_data.len() as f64 - 1.0);
            let lower = index.floor() as usize;
            let upper = index.ceil() as usize;
            if lower == upper {
                sorted_data[lower]
            } else {
                let fraction = index - lower as f64;
                sorted_data[lower] * (1.0 - fraction) + sorted_data[upper] * fraction
            }
        }
        if data.is_empty() {
            return None;
        }
        let mut data = data.clone();
        data.sort_unstable_by_key(|x| OrderedFloat(*x));
        let q1 = percentile(&data, 25.0);
        let q3 = percentile(&data, 75.0);
        let iqr = q3 - q1;
        let upper_bound = q3 + 1.5 * iqr;
        Some(upper_bound)
    }
}

    impl DieSize {
        pub fn bbox_corner(&self) -> ((float, float), (float, float)) {
            (
                (self.x_lower_left, self.y_lower_left),
                (self.x_upper_right, self.y_upper_right),
            )
        }
        pub fn inside(&self, a: (float, float), b: (float, float)) -> bool {
            self.x_lower_left <= a.0 && a.0 <= b.0 && b.0 <= self.x_upper_right
                && self.y_lower_left <= a.1 && a.1 <= b.1 && b.1 <= self.y_upper_right
        }
        pub fn half_perimeter(&self) -> float {
            (self.x_upper_right - self.x_lower_left + self.y_upper_right
                - self.y_lower_left)
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments, clippy::fn_params_excessive_bools)]
        fn __orig_new(
            x_lower_left: float,
            y_lower_left: float,
            x_upper_right: float,
            y_upper_right: float,
        ) -> Self {
            let area = (x_upper_right - x_lower_left) * (y_upper_right - y_lower_left);
            Self {
                x_lower_left,
                y_lower_left,
                x_upper_right,
                y_upper_right,
                area,
            }
        }

    #[allow(deprecated)]
    impl<S: die_size_builder::State> DieSizeBuilder<S> {
        /// Finishes building and performs the requested action.
        #[inline(always)]
        #[allow(
            clippy::inline_always,
            clippy::future_not_send,
            clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
        )]
        pub fn build(self) -> DieSize
        where
            S: die_size_builder::IsComplete,
        {
            let x_lower_left: float = unsafe {
                ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(self.__unsafe_private_named.0)
            };
            let y_lower_left: float = unsafe {
                ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(self.__unsafe_private_named.1)
            };
            let x_upper_right: float = unsafe {
                ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(self.__unsafe_private_named.2)
            };
            let y_upper_right: float = unsafe {
                ::core::option::Option::unwrap_unchecked(self.__unsafe_private_named.3)
            };
            <DieSize>::__orig_new(
                x_lower_left,
                y_lower_left,
                x_upper_right,
                y_upper_right,
            )
        }
        /**_**Required.**_

*/
        #[allow(
            clippy::inline_always,
            clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
            clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
        )]
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn x_lower_left(
            mut self,
            value: float,
        ) -> DieSizeBuilder<die_size_builder::SetXLowerLeft<S>>
        where
            S::XLowerLeft: die_size_builder::IsUnset,
        {
            self.__unsafe_private_named.0 = ::core::option::Option::Some(value);
            DieSizeBuilder {
                __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                __unsafe_private_named: self.__unsafe_private_named,
            }
        }
        /**_**Required.**_

*/
        #[allow(
            clippy::inline_always,
            clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
            clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
        )]
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn y_lower_left(
            mut self,
            value: float,
        ) -> DieSizeBuilder<die_size_builder::SetYLowerLeft<S>>
        where
            S::YLowerLeft: die_size_builder::IsUnset,
        {
            self.__unsafe_private_named.1 = ::core::option::Option::Some(value);
            DieSizeBuilder {
                __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                __unsafe_private_named: self.__unsafe_private_named,
            }
        }
        /**_**Required.**_

*/
        #[allow(
            clippy::inline_always,
            clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
            clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
        )]
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn x_upper_right(
            mut self,
            value: float,
        ) -> DieSizeBuilder<die_size_builder::SetXUpperRight<S>>
        where
            S::XUpperRight: die_size_builder::IsUnset,
        {
            self.__unsafe_private_named.2 = ::core::option::Option::Some(value);
            DieSizeBuilder {
                __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                __unsafe_private_named: self.__unsafe_private_named,
            }
        }
        /**_**Required.**_

*/
        #[allow(
            clippy::inline_always,
            clippy::impl_trait_in_params,
            clippy::missing_const_for_fn,
        )]
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn y_upper_right(
            mut self,
            value: float,
        ) -> DieSizeBuilder<die_size_builder::SetYUpperRight<S>>
        where
            S::YUpperRight: die_size_builder::IsUnset,
        {
            self.__unsafe_private_named.3 = ::core::option::Option::Some(value);
            DieSizeBuilder {
                __unsafe_private_phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
                __unsafe_private_named: self.__unsafe_private_named,
            }
        }
    }
    #[allow(unnameable_types, unreachable_pub, clippy::redundant_pub_crate)]
    /**Tools for manipulating the type state of [`DieSizeBuilder`].

See the [detailed guide](https://bon-rs.com/guide/typestate-api) that describes how all the pieces here fit together.*/
    #[allow(deprecated)]
    mod die_size_builder {
        #[doc(inline)]
        pub use ::bon::__::{IsSet, IsUnset};
        use ::bon::__::{Set, Unset};
        mod sealed {
            pub struct Sealed;
        }
        /**Builder's type state specifies if members are set or not (unset).

You can use the associated types of this trait to control the state of individual members with the [`IsSet`] and [`IsUnset`] traits. You can change the state of the members with the `Set*` structs available in this module.*/
        pub trait State: ::core::marker::Sized {
            /**Type state of the member `x_lower_left`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
            type XLowerLeft;
            /**Type state of the member `y_lower_left`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
            type YLowerLeft;
            /**Type state of the member `x_upper_right`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
            type XUpperRight;
            /**Type state of the member `y_upper_right`.

It can implement either [`IsSet`] or [`IsUnset`]*/
            type YUpperRight;
            #[doc(hidden)]
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed;
        }
        /**Marker trait that indicates that all required members are set.

In this state, you can finish building by calling the method [`DieSizeBuilder::build()`](super::DieSizeBuilder::build())*/
        pub trait IsComplete: State {
            #[doc(hidden)]
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl<S: State> IsComplete for S
        where
            S::XLowerLeft: IsSet,
            S::YLowerLeft: IsSet,
            S::XUpperRight: IsSet,
            S::YUpperRight: IsSet,
        {
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[deprecated = "this should not be used directly; it is an implementation detail; use the Set* type aliases to control the state of members instead"]
        #[doc(hidden)]
        #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
        mod members {
            pub struct x_lower_left(());
            pub struct y_lower_left(());
            pub struct x_upper_right(());
            pub struct y_upper_right(());
        }
        /// Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsUnset`] implemented for all members.
        ///
        /// This is the initial state of the builder before any setters are called.
        pub struct Empty(());
        /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::XLowerLeft`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
        pub struct SetXLowerLeft<S: State = Empty>(
            ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
        );
        /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::YLowerLeft`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
        pub struct SetYLowerLeft<S: State = Empty>(
            ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
        );
        /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::XUpperRight`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
        pub struct SetXUpperRight<S: State = Empty>(
            ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
        );
        /**Represents a [`State`] that has [`IsSet`] implemented for [`State::YUpperRight`].

The state for all other members is left the same as in the input state.*/
        pub struct SetYUpperRight<S: State = Empty>(
            ::core::marker::PhantomData<fn() -> S>,
        );
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl State for Empty {
            type XLowerLeft = Unset<members::x_lower_left>;
            type YLowerLeft = Unset<members::y_lower_left>;
            type XUpperRight = Unset<members::x_upper_right>;
            type YUpperRight = Unset<members::y_upper_right>;
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl<S: State> State for SetXLowerLeft<S> {
            type XLowerLeft = Set<members::x_lower_left>;
            type YLowerLeft = S::YLowerLeft;
            type XUpperRight = S::XUpperRight;
            type YUpperRight = S::YUpperRight;
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl<S: State> State for SetYLowerLeft<S> {
            type XLowerLeft = S::XLowerLeft;
            type YLowerLeft = Set<members::y_lower_left>;
            type XUpperRight = S::XUpperRight;
            type YUpperRight = S::YUpperRight;
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl<S: State> State for SetXUpperRight<S> {
            type XLowerLeft = S::XLowerLeft;
            type YLowerLeft = S::YLowerLeft;
            type XUpperRight = Set<members::x_upper_right>;
            type YUpperRight = S::YUpperRight;
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
        #[doc(hidden)]
        impl<S: State> State for SetYUpperRight<S> {
            type XLowerLeft = S::XLowerLeft;
            type YLowerLeft = S::YLowerLeft;
            type XUpperRight = S::XUpperRight;
            type YUpperRight = Set<members::y_upper_right>;
            const SEALED: sealed::Sealed = sealed::Sealed;
        }
    }
    pub struct Pin {
        pub name: String,
        pub x: float,
        pub y: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Pin {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field3_finish(
                f,
                "Pin",
                "name",
                &self.name,
                "x",
                &self.x,
                "y",
                &&self.y,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Pin {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Pin {
            Pin {
                name: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.name),
                x: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.x),
                y: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.y),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Pin {
        pub fn new(name: String, x: float, y: float) -> Self {
            Self { name, x, y }
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
    }
    pub struct BuildingBlock {
        pub name: String,
        pub width: float,
        pub height: float,
        pub num_pins: uint,
        pub pins: ListMap<String, Pin>,
        pub area: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for BuildingBlock {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            let names: &'static _ = &[
                "name",
                "width",
                "height",
                "num_pins",
                "pins",
                "area",
            ];
            let values: &[&dyn ::core::fmt::Debug] = &[
                &self.name,
                &self.width,
                &self.height,
                &self.num_pins,
                &self.pins,
                &&self.area,
            ];
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_fields_finish(
                f,
                "BuildingBlock",
                names,
                values,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for BuildingBlock {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> BuildingBlock {
            BuildingBlock {
                name: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                width: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                height: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                area: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl BuildingBlock {
        pub fn new(name: String, width: float, height: float, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            let area = width * height;
            let pins = ListMap::default();
            Self {
                name,
                width,
                height,
                num_pins,
                pins,
                area,
            }
        }
    }
    pub struct IOput {
        cell: BuildingBlock,
        is_input: bool,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for IOput {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field2_finish(
                f,
                "IOput",
                "cell",
                &self.cell,
                "is_input",
                &&self.is_input,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for IOput {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> IOput {
            IOput {
                cell: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                is_input: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl IOput {
        pub fn new(is_input: bool) -> Self {
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(String::new(), 0.0, 0.0, 1);
            let mut input = Self { cell: cell, is_input };
            input.cell.pins.push(String::new(), Pin::new(String::new(), 0.0, 0.0));
            input
        }
    }
    pub struct Gate {
        pub cell: BuildingBlock,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Gate {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field1_finish(
                f,
                "Gate",
                "cell",
                &&self.cell,
            )
        }
    }
    impl Gate {
        pub fn new(name: String, width: float, height: float, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(name, width, height, num_pins);
            Self { cell }
        }
    }
    pub struct FlipFlop {
        pub cell: BuildingBlock,
        pub bits: uint,
        pub qpin_delay: float,
        pub power: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for FlipFlop {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "FlipFlop",
                "cell",
                &self.cell,
                "bits",
                &self.bits,
                "qpin_delay",
                &self.qpin_delay,
                "power",
                &&self.power,
            )
        }
    }
    impl FlipFlop {
        pub fn new(
            bits: uint,
            name: String,
            width: float,
            height: float,
            num_pins: uint,
        ) -> Self {
            let power = 0.0;
            let qpin_delay = 0.0;
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(name, width, height, num_pins);
            Self {
                cell: cell,
                bits,
                qpin_delay,
                power,
            }
        }
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<Reference<Pin>> {
            self.cell
                .pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow_mut().name.to_lowercase().starts_with("d"))
                .map(|pin| clone_ref(pin))
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn evaluate_power_area_ratio(&self, mbffg: &MBFFG) -> float {
            (mbffg.power_weight() * self.power + mbffg.area_weight() * self.cell.area)
                / self.bits.float()
        }
        pub fn name(&self) -> &String {
            &self.cell.name
        }
        pub fn width(&self) -> float {
            self.cell.width
        }
        pub fn height(&self) -> float {
            self.cell.height
        }
        /// returns the (width, height) of the flip-flop
        pub fn size(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.width(), self.height())
        }
        /// Calculates the grid coverage of the flip-flop within a given placement row.
        /// Returns a tuple containing the number of grid cells covered in the x and y directions.
        pub fn grid_coverage(&self, placement_row: &PlacementRows) -> (uint, uint) {
            let (width, height) = (placement_row.width, placement_row.height);
            let (w, h) = (self.width(), self.height());
            let (x, y) = ((h / height).ceil(), (w / width).ceil());
            (x.uint(), y.uint())
        }
    }
    pub enum InstType {
        FlipFlop(FlipFlop),
        Gate(Gate),
        IOput(IOput),
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for InstType {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "FlipFlop",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
                InstType::Gate(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "Gate",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
                InstType::IOput(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "IOput",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
            }
        }
    }
    pub trait InstTrait {
        fn property(&mut self) -> &mut BuildingBlock;
        fn property_ref(&self) -> &BuildingBlock;
        fn ff(&mut self) -> &mut FlipFlop;
        fn qpin_delay(&mut self) -> float {
            self.ff().qpin_delay
        }
        fn is_ff(&self) -> bool;
        fn ff_ref(&self) -> &FlipFlop;
    }
    impl InstTrait for InstType {
        fn property(&mut self) -> &mut BuildingBlock {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => &mut flip_flop.cell,
                InstType::Gate(gate) => &mut gate.cell,
                InstType::IOput(ioput) => &mut ioput.cell,
            }
        }
        fn property_ref(&self) -> &BuildingBlock {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => &flip_flop.cell,
                InstType::Gate(gate) => &gate.cell,
                InstType::IOput(ioput) => &ioput.cell,
            }
        }
        fn ff(&mut self) -> &mut FlipFlop {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => flip_flop,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("{0} is Not a flip-flop", self.property().name),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        fn ff_ref(&self) -> &FlipFlop {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => flip_flop,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Not a flip-flop"));
                }
            }
        }
        fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
    }
    pub struct PrevFFRecord {
        pub qpin_delay: float,
        pub ff_q: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub travel_delay: float,
        pub target_pin_id: usize,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for PrevFFRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> PrevFFRecord {
            PrevFFRecord {
                qpin_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.qpin_delay),
                ff_q: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_q),
                travel_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.travel_delay),
                target_pin_id: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.target_pin_id),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for PrevFFRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> PrevFFRecord {
            PrevFFRecord {
                qpin_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                ff_q: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                travel_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                target_pin_id: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Hash for PrevFFRecord {
        fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            match &self.ff_q {
                None => {
                    0.hash(state);
                }
                Some((left, right)) => {
                    left.borrow().id.hash(state);
                    right.borrow().id.hash(state);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    impl PartialEq for PrevFFRecord {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            if self.ff_q.is_none() && other.ff_q.is_none() {
                return true;
            } else if self.ff_q.is_none() || other.ff_q.is_none() {
                return false;
            } else {
                self.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap().0.borrow().id
                    == other.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap().0.borrow().id
                    && self.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap().1.borrow().id
                        == other.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap().1.borrow().id
            }
        }
    }
    impl Eq for PrevFFRecord {}
    impl PrevFFRecord {
        pub fn has_ff_q(&self) -> bool {
            self.ff_q.is_some()
        }
        pub fn ff_q_dist(&self) -> float {
            if let Some((ff_q, _)) = &self.ff_q {
                ff_q.distance(&self.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap().1)
            } else {
                0.0
            }
        }
        pub fn ff_delay(&self, displacement_delay: float) -> float {
            self.qpin_delay + displacement_delay * self.ff_q_dist()
        }
        pub fn travel_delay(&self, displacement_delay: float) -> float {
            displacement_delay * self.travel_delay
        }
        pub fn calculate_total_delay(&self, displacement_delay: float) -> float {
            self.ff_delay(displacement_delay) + self.travel_delay(displacement_delay)
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Debug for PrevFFRecord {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("PrevFFRecord")
                .field("ff_q", &self.ff_q)
                .field("qpin_delay", &round(self.qpin_delay, 2))
                .field("travel_delay", &self.travel_delay)
                .finish()
        }
    }
    pub struct TimingRecord {
        pub ff_q: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub ff_delay: float,
        pub travel_delay: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for TimingRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> TimingRecord {
            TimingRecord {
                ff_q: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                ff_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                travel_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for TimingRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> TimingRecord {
            TimingRecord {
                ff_q: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_q),
                ff_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_delay),
                travel_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.travel_delay),
            }
        }
    }
    impl TimingRecord {
        pub fn total(&self) -> float {
            self.ff_delay + self.travel_delay
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Debug for TimingRecord {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("TimingRecord")
                .field("ff_delay", &round(self.ff_delay, 2))
                .field("travel_delay", &round(self.travel_delay, 2))
                .field("total", &(round(self.total(), 2)))
                .finish()
        }
    }
    static mut PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER: usize = 0;
    pub struct PhysicalPin {
        pub net_name: String,
        pub inst: WeakInst,
        pub pin: WeakReference<Pin>,
        pub pin_name: String,
        pub slack: float,
        origin_pin: Vec<WeakPhysicalPin>,
        pub origin_dist: OnceCell<float>,
        pub merged: bool,
        #[hash]
        pub id: usize,
        pub timing_record: Option<TimingRecord>,
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for PhysicalPin {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            true && self.id == other.id
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for PhysicalPin {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for PhysicalPin {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            self.id.hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct SharedPhysicalPin(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>);
    impl SharedPhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(value: PhysicalPin) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<PhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<PhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            WeakPhysicalPin(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_net_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.net_name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_net_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.net_name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_net_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().net_name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_inst(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakInst> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.inst)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_inst_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakInst> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.inst)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_inst(&self, value: WeakInst) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().inst = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pin(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakReference<Pin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pin_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakReference<Pin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pin(&self, value: WeakReference<Pin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pin = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pin_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pin_name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pin_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pin_name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pin_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pin_name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_slack(&self) -> float {

        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_slack_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<float> {

        }

        pub fn set_slack(&self, value: float) -> &Self {

        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_origin_dist(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<OnceCell<float>> {

        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_origin_dist_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<OnceCell<float>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.origin_dist)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_origin_dist(&self, value: OnceCell<float>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().origin_dist = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_merged(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().merged
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_merged_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.merged)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_merged(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().merged = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_id(&self) -> usize {
            self.borrow().id
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_id_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<usize> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.id)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_id(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().id = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_timing_record(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Option<TimingRecord>> {

        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_timing_record_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Option<TimingRecord>> {
