    impl Clone for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedPhysicalPin").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>> for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<PhysicalPin> for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: PhysicalPin) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedPhysicalPin> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedPhysicalPin) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            *self.0.borrow() == *other.0.borrow()
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for SharedPhysicalPin {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            (&*self.0 as *const _ as usize).hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakPhysicalPin(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>);
    impl WeakPhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedPhysicalPin::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_net_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().net_name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_inst(&self, value: WeakInst) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().inst = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pin(&self, value: WeakReference<Pin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pin = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pin_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pin_name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_slack(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().slack = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_origin_dist(&self, value: OnceCell<float>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().origin_dist = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_merged(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().merged = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_id(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().id = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_timing_record(&self, value: Option<TimingRecord>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().timing_record = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakPhysicalPin")
                .field("is_expired", &self.is_expired())
                .finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>> for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakPhysicalPin> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakPhysicalPin) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl PhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(inst: &SharedInst, pin: &Reference<Pin>) -> Self {
            let inst = inst.downgrade();
            let pin = clone_weak_ref(pin);
            let pin_name = pin.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().name.clone();
            Self {
                net_name: String::new(),
                inst,
                pin,
                pin_name,
                slack: 0.0,
                origin_pin: Vec::new(),
                origin_dist: OnceCell::new(),
                merged: false,
                id: unsafe {
                    PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER += 1;
                    PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER
                },
                timing_record: None,
            }
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> (float, float) {
            let posx = self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().x
                + self.pin.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().x;
            let posy = self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().y
                + self.pin.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().y;
            (posx, posy)
        }
        pub fn x(&self) -> float {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().x
        }
        pub fn y(&self) -> float {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().y
        }
        pub fn inst_name(&self) -> String {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().get_name().clone()
        }
        pub fn full_name(&self) -> String {
            if self.pin_name.is_empty() {
                return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().name.clone();
            } else {
                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                        format_args!("{0}/{1}", self.inst_name(), self.pin_name),
                    );
                    res
                })
            }
        }
        pub fn ori_full_names(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.get_origin_pins().iter().map(|pin| pin.full_name()).collect()
        }
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_ff()
        }
        pub fn is_d_pin(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with('d') || self.pin_name.starts_with('D'));
        }
        pub fn is_q_pin(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with('q') || self.pin_name.starts_with('Q'));
        }
        pub fn is_clk_pin(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("clk")
                    || self.pin_name.starts_with("CLK"));
        }
        pub fn is_gate(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_gt();
        }
        pub fn is_gate_in(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_gt()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("in") || self.pin_name.starts_with("IN"));
        }
        pub fn is_gate_out(&self) -> bool {
            return self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_gt()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("out")
                    || self.pin_name.starts_with("OUT"));
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().lib.borrow() {
                InstType::IOput(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn slack(&self) -> float {
            if !self.is_d_pin() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "{1}{0} is not a D pin{2}",
                            self.full_name(),
                            color_red,
                            color_reset,
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.slack
        }
        pub fn d_pin_slack_total(&self) -> float {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.inst
                .upgrade()
                .unwrap()
                .borrow()
                .dpins()
                .iter()
                .map(|pin| pin.borrow().slack())
                .sum()
        }
        pub fn set_walked(&self, walked: bool) {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().set_walked(walked);
        }
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, highlighted: bool) {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().set_highlighted(highlighted);
        }
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().get_gid()
        }
        pub fn inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().clone()
        }
        pub fn is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().get_is_origin()
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            norm1(self.pos(), other.borrow().pos())
        }
        pub fn distance_to_point(&self, other: &(float, float)) -> float {
            norm1(self.pos(), *other)
        }
        pub fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().lib.borrow().ff_ref().qpin_delay
        }
        pub fn ff_origin_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "{1}{0} is not a flip-flop{2}",
                            self.full_name(),
                            color_red,
                            color_reset,
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.origin_pin[0].upgrade().unwrap()
        }
        pub fn record_origin_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            if !self.is_clk_pin() {
                if !self.origin_pin.is_empty() {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!(
                                "{1}{0} already has an origin pin{2}",
                                self.full_name(),
                                color_red,
                                color_reset,
                            ),
                        );
                    }
                }
            }
            self.origin_pin.push(pin.downgrade());
        }
        pub fn is_empty_bit(&self) -> bool {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.origin_pin.is_empty()
        }
        pub fn get_origin_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            if !self.is_clk_pin() {
                if !(self.origin_pin.len() == 1) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!(
                                "{3}{0} has incorrect #{1} origin pin{4}, {2:?}",
                                self.full_name(),
                                self.origin_pin.len(),
                                self.origin_pin.iter().map(|x| x.full_name()).join(", "),
                                color_red,
                                color_reset,
                            ),
                        );
                    }
                }
            }
            if self.is_origin() {
                return self
                    .origin_pin
                    .iter()
                    .map(|pin| {
                        pin.upgrade()
                            .expect(
                                &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "Pin in {0} has no origin pin",
                                            pin.full_name(),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                    res
                                }),
                            )
                    })
                    .collect();
            } else {
                self.origin_pin
                    .iter()
                    .flat_map(|pin| pin.upgrade().unwrap().get_origin_pins())
                    .collect()
            }
        }
    }
    impl SharedPhysicalPin {
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn pos(&self) -> (float, float) {
            self.0.borrow().pos()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn x(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().x()
        }
        #[inline(always)]

            self.0.borrow().y()
        }

            self.0.borrow().inst_name()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn full_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().full_name()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn ori_full_names(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.0.borrow().ori_full_names()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_ff()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_d_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_d_pin()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_q_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_q_pin()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_clk_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_clk_pin()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_gate(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gate()
        }
        #[inline(always)]

            self.0.borrow().is_gate_in()
        }
        #[inline(always)]

        #[inline(always)]

            self.0.borrow().is_io()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn slack(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().slack()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn d_pin_slack_total(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().d_pin_slack_total()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_walked(&self, walked: bool) {

        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, highlighted: bool) {
            self.0.borrow().set_highlighted(highlighted)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.0.borrow().get_gid()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.0.borrow().inst()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_origin()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().distance(other)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn distance_to_point(&self, other: &(float, float)) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().distance_to_point(other)
        }

            self.0.borrow().qpin_delay()
        }

            self.0.borrow().ff_origin_pin()

            self.0.borrow_mut().record_origin_pin(pin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_empty_bit(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_empty_bit()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_origin_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().get_origin_pins()
        }
    }

    impl fmt::Debug for PhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {

                .field("name", &self.full_name())
                .field("timing", &self.timing_record)
                .finish()
        }

    pub struct Inst {
        pub name: String,
        pub x: float,
        pub y: float,
        pub lib: Reference<InstType>,
        pub libid: int,
        pub pins: ListMap<String, PhysicalPin>,
        pub clk_neighbor: Reference<Vec<String>>,
        pub is_origin: bool,
        pub gid: usize,
        pub walked: bool,
        pub highlighted: bool,
        pub origin_inst: Vec<WeakInst>,
        pub legalized: bool,
        pub optimized_pos: (float, float),
        pub locked: bool,
        /// Indicate that the inst is only partially connected to the netlist
        pub is_orphan: bool,
        pub clk_net: WeakNet,
    }
    pub struct SharedInst(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>);
    impl SharedInst {
        pub fn new(value: Inst) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Inst> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Inst> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakInst {
            WeakInst(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_x(&self) -> float {
            self.borrow().x
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_x_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<float> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.x)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_x(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().x = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_y(&self) -> float {
            self.borrow().y
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_y_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<float> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.y)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_y(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().y = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_lib(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Reference<InstType>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.lib)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_lib_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Reference<InstType>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.lib)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_lib(&self, value: Reference<InstType>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().lib = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_libid(&self) -> int {
            self.borrow().libid
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_libid_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<int> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.libid)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_libid(&self, value: int) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().libid = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pins(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<ListMap<String, PhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pins)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pins_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<ListMap<String, PhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pins)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: ListMap<String, PhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_clk_neighbor(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Reference<Vec<String>>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.clk_neighbor)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_clk_neighbor_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Reference<Vec<String>>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.clk_neighbor)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_clk_neighbor(&self, value: Reference<Vec<String>>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().clk_neighbor = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_origin
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_origin_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_origin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_origin(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_origin = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.borrow().gid
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_gid_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<usize> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.gid)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_gid(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().gid = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_walked(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().walked
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_walked_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.walked)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_walked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().walked = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_highlighted(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().highlighted
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_highlighted_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.highlighted)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().highlighted = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_origin_inst(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Vec<WeakInst>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.origin_inst)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_origin_inst_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Vec<WeakInst>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.origin_inst)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_origin_inst(&self, value: Vec<WeakInst>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().origin_inst = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_legalized(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().legalized
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_legalized_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.legalized)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_legalized(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().legalized = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_optimized_pos(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<(float, float)> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.optimized_pos)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_optimized_pos_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<(float, float)> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.optimized_pos)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_optimized_pos(&self, value: (float, float)) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().optimized_pos = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_locked(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().locked
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_locked_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.locked)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_locked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().locked = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_orphan(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_orphan
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_orphan_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_orphan)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_orphan(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_orphan = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_clk_net(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakNet> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.clk_net)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_clk_net_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakNet> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.clk_net)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_clk_net(&self, value: WeakNet) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().clk_net = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for SharedInst {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedInst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedInst").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>> for SharedInst {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<Inst> for SharedInst {
        fn from(inner: Inst) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedInst> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedInst) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakInst(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>);
    impl WeakInst {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedInst> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedInst::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_x(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().x = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_y(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().y = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_lib(&self, value: Reference<InstType>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().lib = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_libid(&self, value: int) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().libid = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: ListMap<String, PhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_clk_neighbor(&self, value: Reference<Vec<String>>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().clk_neighbor = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_origin(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_origin = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_gid(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().gid = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_walked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().walked = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().highlighted = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_origin_inst(&self, value: Vec<WeakInst>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().origin_inst = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_legalized(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().legalized = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_optimized_pos(&self, value: (float, float)) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().optimized_pos = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_locked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().locked = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_orphan(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_orphan = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_clk_net(&self, value: WeakNet) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().clk_net = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakInst {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakInst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakInst").field("is_expired", &self.is_expired()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>> for WeakInst {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakInst> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakInst) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl Inst {
        pub fn new(name: String, x: float, y: float, lib: &Reference<InstType>) -> Self {
            let pins = ListMap::default();
            let clk_neighbor = build_ref(Vec::new());
            let lib = clone_ref(lib);
            Self {
                name,
                x,
                y,
                lib,
                libid: 0,
                pins,
                clk_neighbor,
                is_origin: true,
                gid: 0,
                walked: false,
                highlighted: false,
                origin_inst: Vec::new(),
                legalized: false,
                optimized_pos: (x, y),
                locked: false,
                is_orphan: false,
                clk_net: Weak::new().into(),
            }
        }
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_gt(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::Gate(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::IOput(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_o(&self) -> bool {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::IOput(x) => !x.is_input,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
        pub fn pos_vec(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
        pub fn move_to(&mut self, x: float, y: float) {
            self.x = x;
            self.y = y;
        }
        pub fn move_to_pos(&mut self, pos: (float, float)) {
            self.x = pos.0;
            self.y = pos.1;
        }
        pub fn move_relative(&mut self, dx: float, dy: float) {
            self.x += dx;
            self.y += dy;
        }
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_d_pin())
                .map(|x| x.clone().into())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn qpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_q_pin())
                .map(|x| x.clone().into())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn unmerged_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| !pin.borrow().merged)
                .map(|x| x.clone().into())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn clkpin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            let mut iter = self.pins.iter().filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_clk_pin());
            let result = iter.next().expect("No clock pin found").clone().into();
            if !iter.next().is_none() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("More than one clk pin"));
                }
            }
            result
        }
        pub fn slack(&self) -> float {
            self.dpins().iter().map(|pin| pin.borrow().slack()).sum()
        }
        pub fn clk_net_name(&self) -> String {
            self.clk_net.upgrade().map(|net| net.get_name().clone()).unwrap_or_default()
        }
        pub fn inpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            if !self.is_gt() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_gt()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_gate_in())
                .map(|pin| pin.borrow().full_name())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn outpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            if !self.is_gt() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_gt()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_gate_out())
                .map(|pin| pin.borrow().full_name())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn center(&self) -> (float, float) {
            let cell = self.lib.borrow();
            (
                self.x + cell.property_ref().width / 2.0,
                self.y + cell.property_ref().height / 2.0,
            )
        }
        pub fn original_center(&self) -> (float, float) {
            cal_center(
                &self.origin_inst.iter().map(|x| x.upgrade().unwrap()).collect_vec(),
            )
        }
        pub fn ll(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.x + 0.1, self.y + 0.1)
        }
        pub fn ur(&self) -> (float, float) {
            let cell = self.lib.borrow();
            (
                self.x + cell.property_ref().width - 0.1,
                self.y + cell.property_ref().height - 0.1,
            )
        }
        pub fn bits(&self) -> uint {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(inst) => inst.bits,
                _ => {
                    #[cold]
                    #[track_caller]
                    #[inline(never)]
                    #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                    #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                    const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                    }
                    panic_cold_display(
                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!("{0} is not a flip-flop", self.name),
                                );
                                res
                            })
                            .red(),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn power(&self) -> float {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(inst) => inst.power,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Not a flip-flop"));
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn width(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().width
        }
        pub fn height(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().height
        }
        pub fn area(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().area
        }
        pub fn bbox(&self) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            let (x, y) = self.pos();
            let (w, h) = (self.width(), self.height());
            let buffer = 0.1;
            [[x + buffer, y + buffer], [x + w - buffer, y + h - buffer]]
        }
        pub fn lib_name(&self) -> String {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().name.clone()
        }
        pub fn assign_lib(&mut self, lib: Reference<InstType>) {
            self.lib = lib;
        }
        pub fn dis_to_origin(&self) -> float {
            norm1(self.center(), self.original_center())
        }
        pub fn origin_insts(&self) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            self.origin_inst.iter().map(|inst| inst.upgrade().unwrap()).collect()
        }
    }
    impl SharedInst {
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_ff()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_gt(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gt()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_io()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn is_o(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_o()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn pos(&self) -> (float, float) {
            self.0.borrow().pos()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn pos_vec(&self) -> (float, float) {
            self.0.borrow().pos_vec()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn move_to(&self, x: float, y: float) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_to(x, y)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn move_to_pos(&self, pos: (float, float)) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_to_pos(pos)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn move_relative(&self, dx: float, dy: float) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_relative(dx, dy)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().dpins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn qpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().qpins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn unmerged_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().unmerged_pins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn clkpin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().clkpin()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn slack(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().slack()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn clk_net_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().clk_net_name()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn inpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.0.borrow().inpins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn outpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.0.borrow().outpins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn center(&self) -> (float, float) {

    impl fmt::Debug for Inst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            let lib_name = if self.is_io() {
                "IOput".to_string()
            } else {
                self.lib.borrow().property_ref().name.clone()
            };
            f.debug_struct("Inst")
                .field("name", &self.name)
                .field("x", &self.x)
                .field("y", &self.y)
                .field("lib", &lib_name)
                .finish()
        }
    }

    impl PlacementRows {
        pub fn get_position(&self, column: i32) -> (float, float) {
            let x = self.x + column as float * self.width;
            let y = self.y;
            (x, y)
        }
    }

    pub struct SharedNet(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>);
    impl SharedNet {
        pub fn new(value: Net) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Net> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Net> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakNet {
            WeakNet(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.name)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pins(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pins)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_pins_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pins)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_clk(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_clk
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn get_is_clk_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_clk)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_clk(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_clk = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for SharedNet {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedNet {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedNet").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>> for SharedNet {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<Net> for SharedNet {
        fn from(inner: Net) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedNet> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedNet) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakNet(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>);
    impl WeakNet {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedNet> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedNet::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn set_is_clk(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_clk = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakNet {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakNet {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakNet").field("is_expired", &self.is_expired()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>> for WeakNet {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakNet> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakNet) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl Net {
        pub fn new(name: String, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            Self {
                name,
                num_pins,
                pins: Vec::new(),
                is_clk: false,
            }
        }
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_clk_pin())
                .cloned()
                .collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.pins.push(pin.clone());
        }
        pub fn remove_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.pins.retain(|p| p.borrow().id != pin.borrow().id);
        }
    }
    impl SharedNet {
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().clock_pins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn add_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().add_pin(pin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn remove_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().remove_pin(pin)
        }
    }
    impl WeakNet {
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().clock_pins()
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn add_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().add_pin(pin)
        }
        #[inline(always)]
        pub fn remove_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().remove_pin(pin)
        }
    }
    pub struct Setting {
        pub alpha: float,
        pub beta: float,
        pub gamma: float,
        pub lambda: float,
        pub die_size: DieSize,
        pub num_input: uint,
        pub num_output: uint,
        pub library: ListMap<String, InstType>,
        pub num_instances: uint,
        pub instances: ListMap<String, Inst>,
        pub num_nets: uint,
        pub nets: Vec<SharedNet>,
        pub physical_pins: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>,
        pub bin_width: float,
        pub bin_height: float,
        pub bin_max_util: float,
        pub placement_rows: Vec<PlacementRows>,
        pub displacement_delay: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Setting {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            let names: &'static _ = &[
                "alpha",
                "beta",
                "gamma",
                "lambda",
                "die_size",
                "num_input",
                "num_output",
                "library",
                "num_instances",
                "instances",
                "num_nets",
                "nets",
                "physical_pins",
                "bin_width",
                "bin_height",
                "bin_max_util",
                "placement_rows",
                "displacement_delay",
            ];
            let values: &[&dyn ::core::fmt::Debug] = &[
                &self.alpha,
                &self.beta,
                &self.gamma,
                &self.lambda,
                &self.die_size,
                &self.num_input,
                &self.num_output,
                &self.library,
                &self.num_instances,
                &self.instances,
                &self.num_nets,
                &self.nets,
                &self.physical_pins,
                &self.bin_width,
                &self.bin_height,
                &self.bin_max_util,
                &self.placement_rows,
                &&self.displacement_delay,
            ];
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_fields_finish(
                f,
                "Setting",
                names,
                values,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for Setting {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Setting {
            Setting {
                alpha: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                beta: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                gamma: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                lambda: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                die_size: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_input: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_output: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                library: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_instances: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                instances: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_nets: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                nets: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                physical_pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_width: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_height: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_max_util: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                placement_rows: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                displacement_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Setting {
        pub fn new(input_path: &str) -> Self {
            let mut setting = Self::read_file(input_path);
            for inst in setting.instances.iter() {
                for pin in inst.borrow().pins.iter() {
                    setting.physical_pins.push(clone_ref(pin).into());
                }
            }
            for pin in setting.physical_pins.iter() {
                pin.borrow_mut().origin_pin.push(pin.downgrade());
            }
            setting
                .placement_rows
                .sort_by_key(|x| (OrderedFloat(x.x), OrderedFloat(x.y)));
            setting
        }
        pub fn read_file(input_path: &str) -> Self {
            let mut setting = Setting::default();
            let file = std::fs::read_to_string(input_path).unwrap();
            let mut instance_state = false;
            for mut line in file.lines() {
                line = line.trim();
                let mut tokens = line.split_whitespace().skip(1);
                if line.starts_with("#") {
                    continue;
                }
                if line.starts_with("Alpha") {
                    setting.alpha = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("Beta") {
                    setting.beta = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("Gamma") {
                    setting.gamma = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("Lambda") {
                    setting.lambda = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("DieSize") {
                    setting.die_size = DieSize::builder()
                        .x_lower_left(tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap())
                        .y_lower_left(tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap())
                        .x_upper_right(tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap())
                        .y_upper_right(tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap())
                        .build();
                } else if line.starts_with("NumInput") {
                    setting.num_input = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<uint>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("Input") || line.starts_with("Output") {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let x = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let y = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let ioput = if line.starts_with("Input") {
                        InstType::IOput(IOput::new(true))
                    } else {
                        InstType::IOput(IOput::new(false))
                    };
                    setting.library.push(name.clone(), ioput);
                    let lib = &setting.library.last().unwrap();
                    let inst = Inst::new(name.clone(), x, y, lib);
                    setting.instances.push(name.clone(), inst);
                    let inst_ref = setting.instances.last().unwrap();
                    inst_ref
                        .borrow_mut()
                        .pins
                        .push(
                            name.clone(),
                            PhysicalPin::new(
                                &inst_ref.clone().into(),
                                &lib.borrow_mut().property().pins[0],
                            ),
                        );
                } else if line.starts_with("NumOutput") {
                    setting.num_output = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("FlipFlop") && !instance_state {
                    let bits = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let width = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    let height = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    let num_pins = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .library
                        .push(
                            name.clone(),
                            InstType::FlipFlop(
                                FlipFlop::new(bits, name.clone(), width, height, num_pins),
                            ),
                        );
                } else if line.starts_with("Gate") && !instance_state {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let width = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    let height = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    let num_pins = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .library
                        .push(
                            name.clone(),
                            InstType::Gate(
                                Gate::new(name.clone(), width, height, num_pins),
                            ),
                        );
                } else if line.starts_with("Pin") && !instance_state {
                    let lib = setting.library.last().unwrap();
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let x = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let y = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    lib.borrow_mut()
                        .property()
                        .pins
                        .push(name.clone(), Pin::new(name, x, y));
                } else if line.starts_with("NumInstances") {
                    setting.num_instances = tokens
                        .next()
                        .unwrap()
                        .parse::<uint>()
                        .unwrap();
                    instance_state = true;
                } else if line.starts_with("Inst") {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let lib_name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let x = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let y = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let lib = setting
                        .library
                        .get(&lib_name)
                        .expect("Library not found!");
                    setting.instances.push(name.clone(), Inst::new(name, x, y, lib));
                    let last_inst = setting.instances.last().unwrap();
                    for lib_pin in lib.borrow_mut().property().pins.iter() {
                        let name = &lib_pin.borrow().name;
                        last_inst
                            .borrow_mut()
                            .pins
                            .push(
                                name.clone(),
                                PhysicalPin::new(&last_inst.clone().into(), lib_pin),
                            );
                    }
                } else if line.starts_with("NumNets") {
                    setting.num_nets = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<uint>().unwrap();
                } else if line.starts_with("Net") {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let num_pins = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<uint>().unwrap();
                    setting.nets.push(SharedNet::new(Net::new(name, num_pins)));
                } else if line.starts_with("Pin") {
                    let pin_token: Vec<&str> = tokens
                        .next()
                        .unwrap()
                        .split("/")
                        .collect();
                    let net_inst = setting.nets.last_mut().unwrap();
                    match pin_token.len() {
                        1 => {
                            let inst_name = pin_token[0].to_string();
                            let pin = &setting
                                .instances
                                .get(&inst_name)
                                .unwrap()
                                .borrow()
                                .pins[0];
                            pin.borrow_mut().net_name = net_inst.borrow().name.clone();
                            net_inst.borrow_mut().pins.push(pin.clone().into());
                        }
                        2 => {
                            let inst_name = pin_token[0].to_string();
                            let pin_name = pin_token[1].to_string();
                            let inst = setting
                                .instances
                                .get(&inst_name)
                                .expect(
                                    ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                format_args!(
                                                    "{2}{0}/{1} is not an instance{3}",
                                                    inst_name,
                                                    pin_name,
                                                    color_red,
                                                    color_reset,
                                                ),
                                            );
                                            res
                                        })
                                        .as_str(),
                                );
                            let pin = clone_ref(
                                inst
                                    .borrow()
                                    .pins
                                    .get(&pin_name)
                                    .expect(
                                        ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                    format_args!(
                                                        "{3}{0}({1}) has no pin named {2}{4}",
                                                        inst_name,
                                                        inst.borrow().lib_name(),
                                                        pin_name,
                                                        color_red,
                                                        color_reset,
                                                    ),
                                                );
                                                res
                                            })
                                            .as_str(),
                                    ),
                            );
                            pin.borrow_mut().net_name = net_inst.borrow().name.clone();
                            if pin.borrow().is_clk_pin() {
                                net_inst.set_is_clk(true);
                                if !inst.borrow().clk_net.upgrade().is_none() {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic(
                                        "assertion failed: inst.borrow().clk_net.upgrade().is_none()",
                                    )
                                }
                                inst.borrow_mut().clk_net = net_inst.downgrade();
                            }
                            net_inst.borrow_mut().pins.push(pin.clone().into());
                        }
                        _ => {
                            {
                                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                    format_args!("Invalid pin name"),
                                );
                            };
                        }
                    }
                } else if line.starts_with("BinWidth") {
                    let value = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting.bin_width = value;
                } else if line.starts_with("BinHeight") {
                    let value = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting.bin_height = value;
                } else if line.starts_with("BinMaxUtil") {
                    let value = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting.bin_max_util = value;
                } else if line.starts_with("PlacementRows") {
                    let x = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let y = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let width = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let height = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    let num_cols = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<int>().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .placement_rows
                        .push(PlacementRows {
                            x,
                            y,
                            width,
                            height,
                            num_cols,
                        });
                } else if line.starts_with("DisplacementDelay") {
                    let value = tokens.next().unwrap().parse().unwrap();
                    setting.displacement_delay = value;
                } else if line.starts_with("QpinDelay") {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let delay = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .library
                        .get(&name)
                        .expect(
                            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                        format_args!("{0} is not in library", name),
                                    );
                                    res
                                })
                                .as_str(),
                        )
                        .borrow_mut()
                        .ff()
                        .qpin_delay = delay;
                } else if line.starts_with("TimingSlack") {
                    let inst_name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let pin_name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let slack = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .instances
                        .get(&inst_name)
                        .expect(
                            &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!("{0} is not in instances", inst_name),
                                );
                                res
                            }),
                        )
                        .borrow_mut()
                        .pins[&pin_name]
                        .borrow_mut()
                        .slack = slack;
                } else if line.starts_with("GatePower") {
                    let name = tokens.next().unwrap().to_string();
                    let power = tokens.next().unwrap().parse::<float>().unwrap();
                    setting
                        .library
                        .get(&name)
                        .expect(
                            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                        format_args!("{0} is not in library", name),
                                    );
                                    res
                                })
                                .as_str(),
                        )
                        .borrow_mut()
                        .ff()
                        .power = power;
                }
            }
            {
                {
                    match (
                        &(setting.num_input.usize() + setting.num_output.usize()),
                        &(setting
                            .instances
                            .iter()
                            .filter(|x| x.borrow().is_io())
                            .count()),
                    ) {
                        (left_val, right_val) => {
                            if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                            ": ",
                                            format_args!("{0}", "Input/Output count is not correct"),
                                            (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            };
            {
                {
                    match (
                        &(setting.num_instances.usize()),
                        &(setting.instances.len() - setting.num_input.usize()
                            - setting.num_output.usize()),
                    ) {
                        (left_val, right_val) => {
                            if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                            ": ",
                                            format_args!(
                                                "{0}",
                                                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                            format_args!(
                                                                "Instances count is not correct: {0}/{1}",
                                                                setting.num_instances,
                                                                setting.instances.len() - setting.num_input.usize()
                                                                    - setting.num_output.usize(),
                                                            ),
                                                        );
                                                        res
                                                    })
                                                    .as_str(),
                                            ),
                                            (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            };
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "NumInput: {0}, NumOutput: {1}, NumInstances: {2}, NumNets: {3}",
                                setting.num_input,
                                setting.num_output,
                                setting.num_instances,
                                setting.num_nets,
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::class",
                                "hello_world::class",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            if setting.num_nets.usize() != setting.nets.len() {
                {
                    {
                        let lvl = ::log::Level::Warn;
                        if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                            ::log::__private_api::log(
                                { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                format_args!(
                                    "NumNets is wrong: ❌ {0} / ✅ {1}",
                                    setting.num_nets,
                                    setting.nets.len(),
                                ),
                                lvl,
                                &(
                                    "hello_world::class",
                                    "hello_world::class",
                                    ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                ),
                                (),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                };
                setting.num_nets = setting.nets.len().u64();
            }
            for net in &setting.nets {
                {
                    {
                        match (
                            &(net.borrow().pins.len()),
                            &(net.borrow().num_pins.usize()),
                        ) {
                            (left_val, right_val) => {
                                if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                    use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                    {
                                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                            format_args!(
                                                "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                                ": ",
                                                format_args!(
                                                    "Net \'{0}\' has {1} pins, but expected {2}",
                                                    net.borrow().name,
                                                    net.borrow().pins.len(),
                                                    net.borrow().num_pins,
                                                ),
                                                (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                            ),
                                        );
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    };
                };
            }
            setting
        }
    }
    pub struct PlacementInfo {
        pub bits: i32,
        pub positions: Vec<(float, float)>,
    }
    impl PlacementInfo {
        ///Constructs a new `PlacementInfo`.
        pub fn new(bits: i32, positions: Vec<(float, float)>) -> Self {
            PlacementInfo {
                bits: bits,
                positions: positions,
            }
        }
    }
    #[doc(hidden)]
    #[allow(non_upper_case_globals, unused_attributes, unused_qualifications)]
    const _: () = {
        #[allow(unused_extern_crates, clippy::useless_attribute)]
        extern crate serde as _serde;
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl _serde::Serialize for PlacementInfo {
            fn serialize<__S>(
                &self,
                __serializer: __S,
            ) -> _serde::__private::Result<__S::Ok, __S::Error>
            where
                __S: _serde::Serializer,
            {
                let mut __serde_state = _serde::Serializer::serialize_struct(
                    __serializer,
                    "PlacementInfo",
                    false as usize + 1 + 1,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::serialize_field(
                    &mut __serde_state,
                    "bits",
                    &self.bits,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::serialize_field(
                    &mut __serde_state,
                    "positions",
                    &self.positions,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::end(__serde_state)
            }
        }
    };
    #[doc(hidden)]
    #[allow(non_upper_case_globals, unused_attributes, unused_qualifications)]
    const _: () = {
        #[allow(unused_extern_crates, clippy::useless_attribute)]
        extern crate serde as _serde;
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl<'de> _serde::Deserialize<'de> for PlacementInfo {
            fn deserialize<__D>(
                __deserializer: __D,
            ) -> _serde::__private::Result<Self, __D::Error>
            where
                __D: _serde::Deserializer<'de>,
            {
                #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
                #[doc(hidden)]
                enum __Field {
                    __field0,
                    __field1,
                    __ignore,
                }
                #[doc(hidden)]
                struct __FieldVisitor;
                #[automatically_derived]
                impl<'de> _serde::de::Visitor<'de> for __FieldVisitor {
                    type Value = __Field;
                    fn expecting(
                        &self,
                        __formatter: &mut _serde::__private::Formatter,
                    ) -> _serde::__private::fmt::Result {
                        _serde::__private::Formatter::write_str(
                            __formatter,
                            "field identifier",
                        )
                    }
                    fn visit_u64<__E>(
                        self,
                        __value: u64,
                    ) -> _serde::__private::Result<Self::Value, __E>
                    where
                        __E: _serde::de::Error,
                    {
                        match __value {
                            0u64 => _serde::__private::Ok(__Field::__field0),
                            1u64 => _serde::__private::Ok(__Field::__field1),
                            _ => _serde::__private::Ok(__Field::__ignore),
                        }
                    }
                    fn visit_str<__E>(

    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for PCell {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field2_finish(
                f,
                "PCell",
                "rect",
                &self.rect,
                "spatial_infos",
                &&self.spatial_infos,
            )
        }
    }
    impl PCell {
        pub fn get(&self, bits: i32) -> Vec<&PlacementInfo> {
            self.spatial_infos.iter().filter(|x| x.bits == bits).collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn filter(&mut self, rtree: &Rtree, (w, h): (float, float)) {
            for placement_info in self.spatial_infos.iter_mut() {
                placement_info
                    .positions
                    .retain(|x| rtree.count([x.0, x.1], [w + x.0, h + x.1]) == 0);
            }
        }
    }
