                .map(|x| &self.graph[x])
                .filter(|x| x.is_ff() && x.get_legalized())
        }
        /// Returns an iterator over all flip-flops (FFs) in the graph.
        pub fn get_all_ffs(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.graph.node_indices().map(|x| &self.graph[x]).filter(|x| x.is_ff())
        }
        pub fn get_all_ff_ids(&self) -> Vec<usize> {
            self.get_all_ffs().map(|x| x.get_gid()).collect_vec()
        }
        fn num_bits(&self) -> uint {
            self.get_all_ffs().map(|x| x.bits()).sum::<uint>() as uint
        }
        pub fn num_ff(&self) -> uint {
            self.get_all_ffs().count() as uint
        }
        pub fn num_nets(&self) -> uint {
            self.setting.nets.len() as uint
        }
        pub fn num_clock_nets(&self) -> uint {
            self.setting.nets.iter().filter(|x| x.borrow().is_clk).count() as uint
        }
        pub fn utilization_score(&self) -> float {
            let bin_width = self.setting.bin_width;
            let bin_height = self.setting.bin_height;
            let bin_max_util = self.setting.bin_max_util;
            let die_size = &self.setting.die_size;
            let col_count = (die_size.x_upper_right / bin_width).round() as uint;
            let row_count = (die_size.y_upper_right / bin_height).round() as uint;
            let mut rtree = Rtree::new();
            rtree.bulk_insert(self.get_all_gates().map(|x| x.bbox()).collect());
            let mut overflow_count = 0.0;
            for i in 0..col_count {
                for j in 0..row_count {
                    let query_box = [
                        [i as float * bin_width, j as float * bin_height],
                        [(i + 1) as float * bin_width, (j + 1) as float * bin_height],
                    ];
                    let query_rect = Rect::new(
                        ::geo_types::Coord {
                            x: query_box[0][0],
                            y: query_box[0][1],
                        },
                        ::geo_types::Coord {
                            x: query_box[1][0],
                            y: query_box[1][1],
                        },
                    );
                    let intersection = rtree.intersection(query_box[0], query_box[1]);
                    let mut overlap_area = 0.0;
                    for ins in intersection {
                        let ins_rect = Rect::new(
                            ::geo_types::Coord {
                                x: ins[0][0],
                                y: ins[0][1],
                            },
                            ::geo_types::Coord {
                                x: ins[1][0],
                                y: ins[1][1],
                            },
                        );
                        overlap_area
                            += query_rect
                                .to_polygon()
                                .intersection(&ins_rect.to_polygon())
                                .unsigned_area();
                    }
                    if overlap_area > bin_height * bin_width * bin_max_util / 100.0 {
                        overflow_count += 1.0;
                    }
                }
            }
            overflow_count
        }
        fn generate_specification_report(&self) -> Table {
            let mut table = Table::new();
            table.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Info".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Value".to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            let num_ffs = self.num_ff();
            let num_gates = self.num_gate();
            let num_ios = self.num_io();
            let num_insts = num_ffs + num_gates;
            let num_nets = self.num_nets();
            let num_clk_nets = self.num_clock_nets();
            let row_count = self.setting.placement_rows.len();
            let col_count = self.setting.placement_rows[0].num_cols;
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#Insts".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_insts.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#FlipFlops".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_ffs.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#Gates".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_gates.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#IOs".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_ios.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#Nets".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_nets.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#ClockNets".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&num_clk_nets.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#Rows".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&row_count.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"#Cols".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&col_count.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table
        }
        pub fn compute_mean_displacement_and_plot(&self) {
            let mut bits_dis = Dict::new();
            for ff in self.get_all_ffs() {
                let pos = ff.pos();
                let supposed_pos = ff.get_optimized_pos().clone();
                let dis = norm1(pos, supposed_pos);
                let bits = ff.bits();
                bits_dis.entry(bits).or_insert(Vec::new()).push(dis);
            }
            {
                ::std::io::_print(format_args!("Mean Displacement:\n"));
            };
            {
                ::std::io::_print(format_args!("------------------\n"));
            };
            for (key, value) in bits_dis.iter() {
                {
                    ::std::io::_print(
                        format_args!("{0}: {1}\n", key, value.mean().int()),
                    );
                };
            }
            {
                ::std::io::_print(format_args!("------------------\n"));
            };
        }
        pub fn compute_mean_shift_and_plot(&self) {
            let mean_shifts = self
                .get_all_ffs()
                .map(|ff| {
                    let origin_inst = ff.get_origin_inst();
                    if origin_inst.is_empty() {
                        return 0.0;
                    }
                    let value = origin_inst
                        .iter()
                        .map(|inst| norm1(inst.center(), ff.original_center()))
                        .collect_vec()
                        .mean();
                    if !!value.is_nan() {
                        {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                format_args!(
                                    "{0:#?} ",
                                    ff
                                        .get_origin_inst()
                                        .iter()
                                        .map(|x| x.upgrade().unwrap().get_name().clone())
                                        .collect_vec(),
                                ),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                    value
                })
                .collect_vec();
            let overall_mean_shift = mean_shifts.mean();
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!("Mean Shift: {0}", overall_mean_shift),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            run_python_script("plot_histogram", (&mean_shifts,));
        }
        pub fn scoring(&mut self, show_specs: bool) -> Score {
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Debug;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!("Scoring..."),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            let mut total_tns = 0.0;
            let mut total_power = 0.0;
            let mut total_area = 0.0;
            let total_utilization = self.utilization_score();
            let mut statistics = Score::default();
            statistics.alpha = self.setting.alpha;
            statistics.beta = self.setting.beta;
            statistics.gamma = self.setting.gamma;
            statistics.lambda = self.setting.displacement_delay;
            statistics.total_count = self.graph.node_count() as uint;
            statistics.io_count = self.num_io();
            statistics.gate_count = self.num_gate();
            statistics.flip_flop_count = self.num_ff();
            if !(statistics.total_count
                == statistics.io_count + statistics.gate_count
                    + statistics.flip_flop_count)
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic(
                    "assertion failed: statistics.total_count ==\n    statistics.io_count + statistics.gate_count + statistics.flip_flop_count",
                )
            }
            self.create_prev_ff_cache();
            for ff in self.get_all_ffs() {
                let slack = self.negative_timing_slack_dp(ff);
                total_tns += slack;
                total_power += ff.power();
                total_area += ff.area();
                (*statistics.bits.entry(ff.bits()).or_default()) += 1;
                statistics.lib.entry(ff.bits()).or_default().insert(ff.lib_name());
                *(statistics.library_usage_count.entry(ff.lib_name()).or_default()) += 1;
            }
            statistics
                .score
                .extend(
                    Vec::from([
                        ("TNS".to_string(), total_tns),
                        ("Power".to_string(), total_power),
                        ("Area".to_string(), total_area),
                        ("Utilization".to_string(), total_utilization),
                    ]),
                );
            let w_tns = total_tns * self.setting.alpha;
            let w_power = total_power * self.setting.beta;
            let w_area = total_area * self.setting.gamma;
            let w_utilization = total_utilization * self.setting.lambda;
            statistics
                .weighted_score
                .extend(
                    Vec::from([
                        ("TNS".to_string(), w_tns),
                        ("Power".to_string(), w_power),
                        ("Area".to_string(), w_area),
                        ("Utilization".to_string(), w_utilization),
                    ]),
                );
            let total_score = w_tns + w_power + w_area + w_utilization;
            statistics
                .ratio
                .extend(
                    Vec::from([
                        ("TNS".to_string(), w_tns / total_score),
                        ("Power".to_string(), w_power / total_score),
                        ("Area".to_string(), w_area / total_score),
                        ("Utilization".to_string(), w_utilization / total_score),
                    ]),
                );
            let mut multibit_storage = Table::new();
            multibit_storage.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
            multibit_storage
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Bits".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Count".to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            for (key, value) in statistics.bits.iter().sorted() {
                multibit_storage
                    .add_row(
                        ::prettytable::Row::new(
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&key.to_string()),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&value.to_string()),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ),
                    );
            }
            let total_ff = self.num_ff();
            if !(statistics.bits.iter().map(|x| x.1).sum::<uint>() == total_ff) {
                ::core::panicking::panic(
                    "assertion failed: statistics.bits.iter().map(|x| x.1).sum::<uint>() == total_ff",
                )
            }
            multibit_storage
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Total".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&total_ff.to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            let mut selection_table = Table::new();
            selection_table.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
            for (key, value) in statistics.lib.iter().sorted_by_key(|x| x.0) {
                let mut value_list = value.iter().cloned().collect_vec();
                value_list.sort_by_key(|x| statistics.library_usage_count[x]);
                value_list.reverse();
                let mut content = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(
                    String::new(),
                    min(value_list.len(), 3),
                );
                selection_table
                    .add_row(
                        ::prettytable::Row::new(
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                    format_args!("* {0}-bits", key),
                                                );
                                                res
                                            })
                                            .as_str()
                                            .to_string(),
                                    ),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ),
                    );
                for lib_group in value_list.chunks(content.len()) {
                    for (i, lib) in lib_group.iter().enumerate() {
                        content[i] = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!(
                                    "{0}:{1}",
                                    lib,
                                    statistics.library_usage_count[lib],
                                ),
                            );
                            res
                        });
                    }
                    selection_table
                        .add_row(
                            Row::new(
                                content
                                    .iter()
                                    .cloned()
                                    .map(|x| prettytable::Cell::new(&x))
                                    .collect(),
                            ),
                        );
                }
            }
            let mut table = Table::new();
            table.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Score".to_string())
                                    .style_spec("bFY"),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Value".to_string())
                                    .style_spec("bFY"),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Weight".to_string())
                                    .style_spec("bFY"),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Weighted Value".to_string())
                                    .style_spec("bFY"),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Ratio".to_string())
                                    .style_spec("bFY"),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            for (key, value) in &statistics
                .score
                .clone()
                .into_iter()
                .sorted_unstable_by_key(|x| Reverse(
                    OrderedFloat(statistics.weighted_score[&x.0]),
                ))
                .collect_vec()
            {
                let weight = match key.as_str() {
                    "TNS" => self.setting.alpha,
                    "Power" => self.setting.beta,
                    "Area" => self.setting.gamma,
                    "Utilization" => self.setting.lambda,
                    _ => 0.0,
                };
                table
                    .add_row(
                        ::prettytable::Row::new(
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&key.to_string()),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&round(*value, 3).to_string()),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&round(weight, 3).to_string()),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &format_with_separator(statistics.weighted_score[key], ',')
                                                .to_string(),
                                        )
                                        .style_spec("r"),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                    format_args!("{0:.1}%", statistics.ratio[key] * 100.0),
                                                );
                                                res
                                            })
                                            .to_string(),
                                    ),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ),
                    );
            }
            let total_score = statistics
                .weighted_score
                .iter()
                .map(|x| x.1)
                .sum::<float>();
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Total".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                    format_args!(
                                                        "{0}\n({1})",
                                                        format_with_separator(total_score, ','),
                                                        scientific_notation(total_score, 2),
                                                    ),
                                                );
                                                res
                                            })
                                            .to_string(),
                                    )
                                    .style_spec("r"),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                    &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                format_args!(
                                                    "{0:.1}%",
                                                    statistics.ratio.iter().map(|x| x.1).sum::<float>() * 100.0,
                                                ),
                                            );
                                            res
                                        })
                                        .to_string(),
                                ),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            table.printstd();
            if show_specs {
                let mut table = Table::new();
                let mut stats_and_selection_table = ::prettytable::Table::init(
                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                            ::prettytable::Row::new(
                                <[_]>::into_vec(
                                    ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Stats".to_string()),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Lib Selection".to_string()),
                                    ]),
                                ),
                            ),
                            ::prettytable::Row::new(
                                <[_]>::into_vec(
                                    ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(&multibit_storage.to_string()),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(&selection_table.to_string()),
                                    ]),
                                ),
                            ),
                        ]),
                    ),
                );
                stats_and_selection_table.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
                table
                    .add_row(
                        ::prettytable::Row::new(
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Specs".to_string())
                                        .style_spec("bFY"),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Multibit Storage".to_string())
                                        .style_spec("bFY"),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ),
                    );
                table
                    .add_row(
                        ::prettytable::Row::new(
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                        &self.generate_specification_report().to_string(),
                                    ),
                                    ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                        &stats_and_selection_table.to_string(),
                                    ),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ),
                    );
                table.printstd();
            }
            statistics
        }
        pub fn output(&self, path: &str) {
            let mut file = File::create(path).unwrap();
            file.write_fmt(format_args!("CellInst {0}\n", self.num_ff())).unwrap();
            let ffs = self.get_all_ffs().collect_vec();
            for inst in ffs.iter() {
                file.write_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "Inst {0} {1} {2} {3}\n",
                            inst.get_name(),
                            inst.lib_name(),
                            inst.pos().0,
                            inst.pos().1,
                        ),
                    )
                    .unwrap();
            }
            for inst in ffs.iter() {
                for pin in inst.get_pins().iter() {
                    if pin.borrow().is_empty_bit() {
                        continue;
                    }
                    let original_full_names = pin.borrow().ori_full_names();
                    if !pin.borrow().is_clk_pin() {
                        if !(original_full_names.len() == 1) {
                            {
                                #[cold]
                                #[track_caller]
                                #[inline(never)]
                                #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                                #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                                const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(
                                    arg: &T,
                                ) -> ! {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                                }
                                panic_cold_display(
                                    &self
                                        .error_message(
                                            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                    format_args!(
                                                        "Pin {0} has multiple original full names: {1:?}",
                                                        pin.borrow().full_name(),
                                                        original_full_names,
                                                    ),
                                                );
                                                res
                                            }),
                                        ),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    for ori_name in original_full_names {
                        file.write_fmt(
                                format_args!(
                                    "{0} map {1}\n",
                                    ori_name,
                                    pin.borrow().full_name(),
                                ),
                            )
                            .unwrap();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn get_lib(&self, lib_name: &str) -> Reference<InstType> {
            self.setting.library.get(&lib_name.to_string()).unwrap().clone()
        }
        pub fn new_ff(
            &mut self,
            name: &str,
            lib: &Reference<InstType>,
            is_origin: bool,
            add_to_graph: bool,
        ) -> SharedInst {
            let inst = SharedInst::new(Inst::new(name.to_string(), 0.0, 0.0, lib));
            for lib_pin in lib.borrow_mut().property().pins.iter() {
                let name = &lib_pin.borrow().name;
                inst.borrow_mut()
                    .pins
                    .push(name.clone(), PhysicalPin::new(&inst, lib_pin));
            }
            inst.set_is_origin(is_origin);
            self.current_insts.insert(inst.get_name().clone(), inst.clone());
            if add_to_graph {
                let node = self.graph.add_node(inst.clone());
                inst.set_gid(node.index());
            }
            inst
        }
        /// Checks if the given instance is a flip-flop (FF) and is present in the current instances.
        /// If not, it asserts with an error message.
        fn check_valid(&self, inst: &SharedInst) {
            if !self.current_insts.contains_key(&inst.borrow().name) {
                {
                    #[cold]
                    #[track_caller]
                    #[inline(never)]
                    #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                    #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                    const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                    }
                    panic_cold_display(
                        &self
                            .error_message(
                                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                        format_args!("Inst {0} not in the graph", inst.get_name()),
                                    );
                                    res
                                }),
                            ),
                    );
                }
            }
            if !inst.is_ff() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Inst {0} is not a FF", inst.get_name()),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn bank(
            &mut self,
            ffs: Vec<SharedInst>,
            lib: &Reference<InstType>,
        ) -> SharedInst {
            self.structure_change = true;
            if !!ffs.is_empty() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: !ffs.is_empty()")
            }
            if !(ffs.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).sum::<u64>() <= lib.borrow().ff_ref().bits)
            {
                {
                    #[cold]
                    #[track_caller]
                    #[inline(never)]
                    #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                    #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                    const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                    }
                    panic_cold_display(
                        &self
                            .error_message(
                                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "FF bits not match: {0} > {1}(lib), [{2}], [{3}]",
                                            ffs.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).sum::<u64>(),
                                            lib.borrow().ff_ref().bits,
                                            ffs.iter().map(|x| x.get_name()).join(", "),
                                            ffs.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).join(", "),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                    res
                                }),
                            ),
                    );
                }
            }
            if !(ffs.iter().map(|x| x.clk_net_name()).collect::<Set<_>>().len() == 1) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("FF clk net not match"));
                }
            }
            ffs.iter().for_each(|x| self.check_valid(x));
            let new_name = ffs.iter().map(|x| x.borrow().name.clone()).join("_");
            let new_inst = self.new_ff(&new_name, &lib, false, true);
            new_inst.get_origin_inst_mut().extend(ffs.iter().map(|x| x.downgrade()));
            if self.debug {
                let message = ffs.iter().map(|x| x.get_name()).join(", ");
                {
                    {
                        let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                        if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                            ::log::__private_api::log(
                                { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                format_args!(
                                    "Banking [{0}] to [{1}]",
                                    message,
                                    new_inst.get_name(),
                                ),
                                lvl,
                                &(
                                    "hello_world::mbffg",
                                    "hello_world::mbffg",
                                    ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                ),
                                (),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                };
            }
            let new_inst_d = new_inst.dpins();
            let new_inst_q = new_inst.qpins();
            let mut d_idx = 0;
            let mut q_idx = 0;
            let clk_net = ffs[0].get_clk_net();
            new_inst.set_clk_net(clk_net.clone());
            clk_net.add_pin(&new_inst.clkpin());
            for ff in ffs.iter() {
                for dpin in ff.dpins().iter() {
                    self.transfer_edge(dpin, &new_inst_d[d_idx]);
                    d_idx += 1;
                }
                for qpin in ff.qpins().iter() {
                    self.transfer_edge(qpin, &new_inst_q[q_idx]);
                    q_idx += 1;
                }
                self.transfer_edge(&ff.clkpin(), &new_inst.clkpin());
                clk_net.remove_pin(&ff.clkpin());
            }
            for ff in ffs.iter() {
                self.remove_ff(ff);
            }
            self.current_insts.insert(new_inst.get_name().clone(), new_inst.clone());
            let new_pos = cal_center(&ffs);
            new_inst.move_to(new_pos.0, new_pos.1);
            new_inst.set_optimized_pos(new_pos);
            new_inst
        }
        pub fn debank(&mut self, inst: &SharedInst) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            self.structure_change = true;
            self.check_valid(inst);
            if !(inst.bits() != 1) {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: inst.bits() != 1")
            }
            if !inst.get_is_origin() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: inst.get_is_origin()")
            }
            let one_bit_lib = self.find_best_library_by_bit_count(1);
            let inst_clk_net = inst.get_clk_net();
            let mut debanked = Vec::new();
            for i in 0..inst.bits() {
                let new_name = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                        format_args!("{0}-{1}", inst.get_name(), i),
                    );
                    res
                });
                let new_inst = self.new_ff(&new_name, &one_bit_lib, false, true);
                new_inst.get_origin_inst_mut().push(inst.downgrade());
                new_inst.move_to_pos(inst.pos());
                inst_clk_net.add_pin(&new_inst.clkpin());
                new_inst.set_clk_net(inst_clk_net.clone());
                let dpin = &inst.dpins()[i.usize()];
                let new_dpin = &new_inst.dpins()[0];
                self.transfer_edge(dpin, new_dpin);
                let qpin = &inst.qpins()[i.usize()];
                let new_qpin = &new_inst.qpins()[0];
                self.transfer_edge(qpin, new_qpin);
                self.transfer_edge(&inst.clkpin(), &new_inst.clkpin());
                self.current_insts.insert(new_inst.get_name().clone(), new_inst.clone());
                debanked.push(new_inst);
            }
            inst_clk_net.remove_pin(&inst.clkpin());
            self.remove_ff(inst);
            debanked
        }
        pub fn transfer_edge(
            &mut self,
            pin_from: &SharedPhysicalPin,
            pin_to: &SharedPhysicalPin,
        ) {
            pin_to.record_origin_pin(pin_from);
            if pin_from.is_clk_pin() || pin_to.is_clk_pin() {
                if !(pin_from.is_clk_pin() && pin_to.is_clk_pin()) {
                    {
                        #[cold]
                        #[track_caller]
                        #[inline(never)]
                        #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                        #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                        const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(
                            arg: &T,
                        ) -> ! {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                        }
                        panic_cold_display(
                            &self
                                .error_message(
                                    "Cannot transfer edge between non-clock and clock pins"
                                        .to_string(),
                                ),
                        );
                    }
                }
            } else {
                let clk_name_from = pin_from.inst().clk_net_name();
                let clk_name_to = pin_to.inst().clk_net_name();
                let same_nonempty_clk = match (
                    clk_name_from.as_str(),
                    clk_name_to.as_str(),
                ) {
                    ("", _) | (_, "") => true,
                    _ => clk_name_from == clk_name_to,
                };
                if !same_nonempty_clk {
                    {
                        #[cold]
                        #[track_caller]
                        #[inline(never)]
                        #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                        #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                        const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(
                            arg: &T,
                        ) -> ! {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                        }
                        panic_cold_display(
                            &self
                                .error_message(
                                    ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                            format_args!(
                                                "Clock net name not match: {0} != {1}",
                                                clk_name_from,
                                                clk_name_to,
                                            ),
                                        );
                                        res
                                    }),
                                ),
                        );
                    }
                }
                self.structure_change = true;
                let inst_from = pin_from.inst();
                let inst_to = pin_to.inst();
                let mut tmp = Vec::new();
                let current_gid = NodeIndex::new(inst_from.get_gid());
                if pin_from.is_d_pin() {
                    let incoming_edges = self
                        .graph
                        .edges_directed(current_gid, Direction::Incoming);
                    for edge in incoming_edges {
                        let weight = edge.weight();
                        if weight.1.get_id() != pin_from.get_id() {
                            continue;
                        }
                        let source = edge.source();
                        let target = NodeIndex::new(inst_to.get_gid());
                        let new_weight = (weight.0.clone(), pin_to.clone());
                        tmp.push((source, target, new_weight));
                    }
                    pin_to.set_slack(pin_from.get_slack());
                    pin_to
                        .get_origin_dist()
                        .set(
                            *pin_from
                                .get_origin_dist()
                                .get()
                                .expect("Origin distance not set"),
                        )
                        .expect("Failed to set origin distance");
                } else if pin_from.is_q_pin() {
                    let outgoing_edges = self
                        .graph
                        .edges_directed(current_gid, Direction::Outgoing)
                        .collect_vec();
                    for edge in outgoing_edges {
                        let weight = edge.weight();
                        if weight.0.get_id() != pin_from.get_id() {
                            continue;
                        }
                        let source = NodeIndex::new(inst_to.get_gid());
                        let target = edge.target();
                        let new_weight = (pin_to.clone(), weight.1.clone());
                        tmp.push((source, target, new_weight));
                    }
                }
                for (source, target, weight) in tmp.into_iter() {
                    self.graph.add_edge(source, target, weight);
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn existing_gate(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.graph.node_indices().map(|x| &self.graph[x]).filter(|x| x.is_gt())
        }
        pub fn existing_io(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.graph.node_indices().map(|x| &self.graph[x]).filter(|x| x.is_io())
        }
        pub fn visualize_layout(
            &self,
            display_in_shell: bool,
            plotly: bool,
            extra_visuals: Vec<PyExtraVisual>,
            file_name: &str,
            bits: Option<Vec<usize>>,
        ) {
            let ffs = if bits.is_none() {
                self.get_all_ffs().collect_vec()
            } else {
                self.get_all_ffs()
                    .filter(|x| bits.as_ref().unwrap().contains(&x.bits().usize()))
                    .collect_vec()
            };
            if !plotly {
                Python::with_gil(|py| {
                        let script = ::pyo3_ffi::_cstr_from_utf8_with_nul_checked(
                            "import math\nimport sys\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nfrom pprint import pprint\nfrom types import SimpleNamespace\n\nimport gurobipy as gp\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nimport pandas as pd\nimport scipy\nimport scipy.spatial\n\n# import scipy.stats\nimport seaborn as sns\nfrom gurobipy import GRB, Model, quicksum\nfrom sklearn.cluster import KMeans\n\nsys.path.append(\"src\")\n\nimport cv2\nimport numpy as np\nfrom gurobi import *\nfrom mindmap import draw_mindmap\nfrom plot import *\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\nfrom utility_image_wo_torch import *\n\n\ndef draw_layout(\n    display_in_shell,\n    file_name,\n    die_size,\n    bin_width,\n    bin_height,\n    placement_rows,\n    flip_flops,\n    gates,\n    io_pins,\n    extra_visual_elements,\n):\n    BORDER_COLOR = (46, 117, 181)\n    PLACEROW_COLOR = (0, 111, 162)\n    FLIPFLOP_COLOR = (165, 226, 206)\n    FLIPFLOP_WALKED_COLOR = (255, 255, 0)\n    FLIPFLOP_OUTLINE_COLOR = (84, 90, 88)\n    GATE_COLOR = (237, 125, 49)\n    GATE_WALKED_COLOR = (0, 0, 255)\n    IO_PIN_OUTLINE_COLOR = (54, 151, 217)\n    DRAW_PLACEMENT_ROWS = False\n    img_width = die_size.x_upper_right\n    img_height = die_size.y_upper_right\n    max_length = 8000\n    ratio = max_length / max(img_width, img_height)\n    img_width, img_height = int(img_width * ratio), int(img_height * ratio)\n    img = np.full((img_height, img_width, 3), 255, np.uint8)\n    border_width = int(max_length * 0.02)\n    # line_width = int(max_length * 0.003)\n    dash_length = int(max_length * 0.01)\n\n    # Draw shaded bins\n    for i in range(0, math.ceil(die_size.x_upper_right / bin_width)):\n        for j in range(0, math.ceil(die_size.y_upper_right / bin_height)):\n            if i % 2 == 0:\n                if j % 2 == 1:\n                    continue\n            elif j % 2 == 0:\n                continue\n            start = (i * bin_width * ratio, j * bin_height * ratio)\n            end = ((i + 1) * bin_width * ratio, (j + 1) * bin_height * ratio)\n            start = np.int32(start)\n            end = np.int32(end)\n            x, y, w, h = start[0], start[1], end[0] - start[0], end[1] - start[1]\n            sub_img = img[y : y + h, x : x + w]\n            white_rect = np.full(sub_img.shape, (120, 120, 120), dtype=np.uint8)\n            res = cv2.addWeighted(sub_img, 0.5, white_rect, 0.5, 0)\n            img[y : y + h, x : x + w] = res\n\n    # Draw the placement rows\n    if DRAW_PLACEMENT_ROWS:\n        dash_line_width = int(abs(placement_rows[0].y - placement_rows[1].y) * ratio / 2.5)\n        dash_length = int(placement_rows[0].width * ratio) * 3\n        bin_site_ratio = bin_height // placement_rows[0].height\n        for row_idx, placement_row in enumerate(placement_rows):\n            x, y = placement_row.x, placement_row.y\n            w = bin_width\n            h = placement_row.height\n            x, y, w, h = int(x * ratio), int(y * ratio), int(w * ratio), int(h * ratio)\n            dashed_line(\n                img,\n                (x, y),\n                (x + w, y),\n                PLACEROW_COLOR,\n                dash_line_width,\n                dash_length=dash_length,\n                gap_length=dash_length,\n            )\n            if row_idx > bin_site_ratio:\n                break\n            # for i in range(1, placement_row.num_cols):\n            #     x = placement_row.x + i * placement_row.width\n            #     x = int(x * ratio)\n            #     dashed_line(\n            #         img,\n            #         (x, y),\n            #         (x, y + h),\n            #         PLACEROW_COLOR,\n            #         line_width,\n            #         dash_length=dash_length,\n            #         gap_length=int(dash_length / 1.5),\n            #     )\n\n    # Draw the flip-flops\n    highlighted_cell = []\n    for ff in flip_flops:\n        x, y = ff.x, ff.y\n        w = ff.width\n        h = ff.height\n        x, y = int(x * ratio), int(y * ratio)\n        w, h = int(w * ratio), int(h * ratio)\n        half_border_width = max(max(w, h) // 70, 1)\n        cv2.rectangle(\n            img,\n            (x + half_border_width, y + half_border_width),\n            (x + w - half_border_width, y + h - half_border_width),\n            FLIPFLOP_COLOR if not ff.walked else FLIPFLOP_WALKED_COLOR,\n            -1,\n        )\n        cv2.rectangle(img, (x, y), (x + w, y + h), FLIPFLOP_OUTLINE_COLOR, half_border_width * 2)\n        if ff.highlighted:\n            highlighted_cell.append((x, y, w, h, half_border_width))\n\n    # centers = km.cluster_centers_\n    cluster_sizes = np.bincount(labels)\n    if method == 0:\n        for cluster_id in range(max(labels) + 1):\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[np.where(cluster_sizes >= 4)] = np.inf\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 1:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # print(\"--\")\n                # print(cluster_sizes[cluster_id])\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[walked_id] = np.inf\n                # print(walked_id)\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n                # print(new_cluster_id)\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 2:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = scipy.spatial.distance.cdist(points[cluster_points], centers)\n                distances[:, walked_id] = np.inf\n                selected_idx, new_cluster_id = np.unravel_index(\n                    np.argmin(distances), distances.shape\n                )\n                cheapest_point_idx = cluster_points[selected_idx]\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    for i in range(len(km.cluster_centers_)):\n        km.cluster_centers_[i] = np.mean(points[np.where(labels == i)], axis=0)\n\n    return km\n\n\ndef evaluate(points, centers, labels, output=False):\n    km_obj = 0\n    for i, point in enumerate(points):\n        km_obj += np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(centers[labels[i]]))\n    if output:\n        print(\"objective value:\", km_obj)\n    return km_obj\n\n\ndef plot_points_with_centers(points, centers, labels, colors):\n    plt.figure()\n model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s centers = km.cluster_centers_\n    cluster_sizes = np.bincount(labels)\n    if method == 0:\n        for cluster_id in range(max(labels) + 1):\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[np.where(cluster_sizes >= 4)] = np.inf\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 1:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # print(\"--\")\n                # print(cluster_sizes[cluster_id])\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[walked_id] = np.inf\n                # print(walked_id)\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n                # print(new_cluster_id)\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 2:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = scipy.spatial.distance.cdist(points[cluster_points], centers)\n                distances[:, walked_id] = np.inf\n                selected_idx, new_cluster_id = np.unravel_index(\n                    np.argmin(distances), distances.shape\n                )\n                cheapest_point_idx = cluster_points[selected_idx]\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    for i in range(len(km.cluster_centers_)):\n        km.cluster_centers_[i] = np.mean(points[np.where(labels == i)], axis=0)\n\n    return km\n\n\ndef evaluate(points, centers, labels, output=False):\n    km_obj = 0\n    for i, point in enumerate(points):\n        km_obj += np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(centers[labels[i]]))\n    if output:\n        print(\"objective value:\", km_obj)\n    return km_obj\n\n\ndef plot_points_with_centers(points, centers, labels, colors):\n    plt.figure()\n gurobipy as gp\n    from gurobipy import GRB\n\n    spatial_occupancy = np.asarray(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(\"grid_size:\", grid_size)\n    # print(\"tiles:\", tiles)\n    # in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s within the bounds of any tile placement\n            model.addConstr(\n                y[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                )\n                + spatial_occupancy[i][j],\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n            model.addConstr(\n                y_weight[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c] / tiles_area[k] * tiles_weight[k]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                ),\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n\n    # Non-overlapping constraints: Each cell can be covered by at most one tile\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            model.addConstr(y[i, j] <= 1, name=f\"no_overlap_{i}_{j}\")\n\n    # Tile count limits\n    if len(tile_limits) > 0:\n        for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n            model.addConstr(\n                gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)) <= tile_limits[k],\n                name=f\"tile_limit_{k}\",\n            )\n\n    # Objective: Maximize total coverage\n    # model.setObjective(gp.quicksum(y[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE)\n    model.setObjective(\n        gp.quicksum(y_weight[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE\n    )\n\n    # Solve the model\n    model.optimize()\n    # Print solution\n    if model.status == GRB.OPTIMAL:\n        # print(\"Optimal solution found!\")\n        # for k, in range(len(capcaity)))/(grid_size[0] * grid_size[1])}\"\n            )\n\n        return capcaity\n    else:\n        print(\"No solution found.\")\n\n\ndef plot_pareto_curve(values, title=\"\",         pub fn check(&self, output_name: &str) {
            fn report_score_from_log(mbffg: &MBFFG, text: &str) {
                let re = Regex::new(
                        r"area change to (\d+)\n.*timing changed to ([\d.]+)\n.*power changed to ([\d.]+)",
                    )
                    .unwrap();
                if let Some(caps) = re.captures(text) {
                    let area: f64 = caps.get(1).unwrap().as_str().parse().unwrap();
                    let timing: f64 = caps.get(2).unwrap().as_str().parse().unwrap();
                    let power: f64 = caps.get(3).unwrap().as_str().parse().unwrap();
                    let score = mbffg.calculate_score(timing, power, area);
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!("Score: {0}", score),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                } else {
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Warn;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!("No score found in the log text"),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                }
            }
            let command = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                    format_args!(
                        "../tools/checker/main {0} {1}",
                        self.input_path,
                        output_name,
                    ),
                );
                res
            });
            self.print_normal_message(
                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                        format_args!("Run command: {0}", command),
                    );
                    res
                }),
            );
            let output = Command::new("bash")
                .arg("-c")
                .arg(command)
                .output()
                .expect("failed to execute process");
            let output_string = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout);
            {
                ::std::io::_print(
                    format_args!("{0}Stdout:\n{1}", color_green, color_reset),
                );
            };
            output_string
                .split("\n")
                .filter(|x| {
                    !x.starts_with("timing change on pin") || !self.filter_timing
                })
                .for_each(|x| {
                    ::std::io::_print(format_args!("{0}\n", x));
                });
            {
                ::std::io::_print(
                    format_args!(
                        "{1}Stderr:\n{2}{0}\n",
                        String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stderr),
                        color_green,
                        color_reset,
                    ),
                );
            };
            report_score_from_log(self, &String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stderr));
        }
        fn clock_nets(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedNet> {
            self.setting.nets.iter().filter(|x| x.borrow().is_clk)
        }
        pub fn get_clock_groups(&self) -> Vec<Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            let clock_nets = self.clock_nets();
            clock_nets
                .map(|x| {
                    x.clock_pins()
                        .into_iter()
                        .filter(|x| !x.inst().borrow().locked)
                        .collect_vec()
                })
                .collect_vec()
        }
        fn pareto_front(&mut self) {
            let library_flip_flops: Vec<_> = self
                .setting
                .library
                .iter()
                .filter(|x| x.borrow().is_ff())
                .collect();
            struct ParetoElement {
                index: usize,
                power: float,
                area: float,
                width: float,
                height: float,
            }
            #[automatically_derived]
            impl ::core::marker::StructuralPartialEq for ParetoElement {}
            #[automatically_derived]
            impl ::core::cmp::PartialEq for ParetoElement {
                #[inline]
                fn eq(&self, other: &ParetoElement) -> bool {
                    self.index == other.index && self.power == other.power
                        && self.area == other.area && self.width == other.width
                        && self.height == other.height
                }
            }
            impl Dominate for ParetoElement {
                /// returns `true` is `self` is better than `x` on all fields that matter to us
                fn dominate(&self, x: &Self) -> bool {
                    (self != x) && (self.power <= x.power && self.area <= x.area)
                        && (self.width <= x.width && self.height <= x.height)
                }
            }
            let frontier: ParetoFront<ParetoElement> = library_flip_flops
                .iter()
                .enumerate()
                .map(|x| {
                    let bits = x.1.borrow().ff_ref().bits as float;
                    ParetoElement {
                        index: x.0,
                        power: x.1.borrow().ff_ref().power / bits,
                        area: x.1.borrow().ff_ref().cell.area / bits,
                        width: x.1.borrow().ff_ref().cell.width,
                        height: x.1.borrow().ff_ref().cell.height,
                    }
                })
                .collect();
            let frontier = frontier.iter().collect_vec();
            let mut result = Vec::new();
            for x in frontier.iter() {
                result.push(library_flip_flops[x.index].clone());
            }
            result
                .sort_by_key(|x| {
                    (
                        x.borrow().ff_ref().bits,
                        OrderedFloat(x.borrow().ff_ref().evaluate_power_area_ratio(self)),
                    )
                });
            for r in 0..result.len() {
                self.library_anchor.insert(result[r].borrow().ff_ref().bits, r);
            }
            self.pareto_library = result;
        }
        pub fn retrieve_ff_libraries(&self) -> &Vec<Reference<InstType>> {
            if !(self.pareto_library.len() > 0) {
                ::core::panicking::panic(
                    "assertion failed: self.pareto_library.len() > 0",
                )
            }
            return &self.pareto_library;
        }
        pub fn print_library(&self, filtered: bool) {
            let mut table = Table::new();
            table.set_format(*format::consts::FORMAT_BOX_CHARS);
            table
                .add_row(
                    ::prettytable::Row::new(
                        <[_]>::into_vec(
                            ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Name".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Bits".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Power".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Area".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Width".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Height".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"Qpin Delay".to_string()),
                                ::prettytable::Cell::new(&"PA_Score".to_string()),
                            ]),
                        ),
                    ),
                );
            let libs = if filtered {
                &self.pareto_library
            } else {
                &self
                    .setting
                    .library
                    .values()
                    .filter(|x| x.borrow().is_ff())
                    .cloned()
                    .collect_vec()
            };
            libs.iter()
                .for_each(|x| {
                    table
                        .add_row(
                            ::prettytable::Row::new(
                                <[_]>::into_vec(
                                    ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().cell.name.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().bits.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().power.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().cell.area.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().cell.width.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &x.borrow().ff_ref().cell.height.to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &round(x.borrow().ff_ref().qpin_delay, 1).to_string(),
                                        ),
                                        ::prettytable::Cell::new(
                                            &round(
                                                    x.borrow().ff_ref().evaluate_power_area_ratio(&self),
                                                    1,
                                                )
                                                .to_string(),
                                        ),
                                    ]),
                                ),
                            ),
                        );
                });
            table.printstd();
        }
        pub fn next_library(&mut self, bits: uint) -> Reference<InstType> {
            let index = self.library_anchor[&bits];
            if index + 1 >= self.pareto_library.len() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("No more library"));
                };
            }
            self.pareto_library[index + 1].clone()
        }
        pub fn best_library(&self) -> Reference<InstType> {
            let start_bit = self.pareto_library[0].borrow().ff_ref().bits;
            let mut lib = self.pareto_library[0].clone();
            let mut i = self.library_anchor[&start_bit];
            while i + 1 < self.pareto_library.len() {
                lib = self.pareto_library[i + 1].clone();
                let bits = lib.borrow().ff_ref().bits;
                i = self.library_anchor[&bits];
            }
            lib
        }
        pub fn find_best_library_by_bit_count(&self, bits: uint) -> Reference<InstType> {
            for lib in self.pareto_library.iter() {
                if lib.borrow().ff_ref().bits == bits {
                    return lib.clone();
                }
            }
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!("No library found for bits {0}", bits),
                );
            };
        }
        pub fn generate_occupancy_map(
            &self,
            include_ff: Option<Vec<uint>>,
            split: i32,
        ) -> (Vec<Vec<bool>>, Vec<Vec<(float, float)>>) {
            let mut rtree = Rtree::new();
            let locked_ffs = self
                .get_free_ffs()
                .filter(|x| x.borrow().locked)
                .map(|x| x.bbox());
            if include_ff.is_some() {
                let gates = self.existing_gate().map(|x| x.bbox());
                let ff_list = include_ff.unwrap().into_iter().collect::<Set<_>>();
                let ffs = self
                    .get_free_ffs()
                    .filter(|x| ff_list.contains(&x.bits()))
                    .map(|x| x.bbox());
                rtree.bulk_insert(gates.chain(ffs).chain(locked_ffs).collect());
            } else {
                rtree
                    .bulk_insert(
                        self
                            .existing_gate()
                            .map(|x| x.bbox())
                            .chain(locked_ffs)
                            .collect(),
                    );
            }
            let mut status_occupancy_map = Vec::new();
            let mut pos_occupancy_map = Vec::new();
            for i in 0..self.setting.placement_rows.len() {
                let placement_row = &self.setting.placement_rows[i];
                let row_height = placement_row.height / split.float();
                for k in 0..split {
                    let mut status_occupancy_row = Vec::new();
                    let mut pos_occupancy_row = Vec::new();
                    let shift = row_height * k.float();
                    let row_bbox = [
                        [placement_row.x, placement_row.y + shift],
                        [
                            placement_row.x
                                + placement_row.width * placement_row.num_cols.float(),
                            placement_row.y + row_height + shift,
                        ],
                    ];
                    let row_intersection = rtree.intersection(row_bbox[0], row_bbox[1]);
                    let mut row_rtee = Rtree::new();
                    row_rtee.bulk_insert(row_intersection);
                    for j in 0..placement_row.num_cols {
                        let x = placement_row.x + j as float * placement_row.width;
                        let y = placement_row.y;
                        let bbox = [
                            [x, y],
                            [x + placement_row.width, y + placement_row.height],
                        ];
                        let is_occupied = row_rtee.count(bbox[0], bbox[1]) > 0;
                        status_occupancy_row.push(is_occupied);
                        pos_occupancy_row.push((x, y));
                    }
                    status_occupancy_map.push(status_occupancy_row);
                    pos_occupancy_map.push(pos_occupancy_row);
                }
            }
            (status_occupancy_map, pos_occupancy_map)
        }
        fn cal_mean_dis(group: &Vec<SharedInst>) -> float {
            if group.len() == 1 {
                return 0.0;
            }
            let center = cal_center(group);
            let mut dis = 0.0;
            for inst in group.iter() {
                dis += norm1(center, inst.center());
            }
            dis
        }
        /// Clusters clock pins into groups using K-means clustering and calculates the mean distance for each group.
        pub fn group_clock_instances_by_kmeans(
            &mut self,
            clock_pins_groups: Vec<Vec<SharedInst>>,
        ) -> Vec<(Vec<SharedInst>, f64)> {
            let cluster_analysis_results = clock_pins_groups
                .iter()
                .map(|clock_pins| {
                    let samples: Vec<f64> = clock_pins
                        .iter()
                        .flat_map(|pin| [pin.get_x(), pin.get_y()])
                        .collect();
                    let num_samples = samples.len() / 2;
                    let samples_np = Array2::from_shape_vec((num_samples, 2), samples)
                        .expect("Invalid shape");
                    let n_clusters = ((num_samples as f64) / 4.0).ceil() as usize;
                    let clustering_result = scipy::cluster::kmeans()
                        .n_clusters(n_clusters)
                        .samples(samples_np)
                        .n_init(1)
                        .call();
                    (clock_pins, clustering_result)
                })
                .tqdm()
                .collect_vec();
            let clustered_instances_with_distance = cluster_analysis_results
                .into_iter()
                .flat_map(|(clock_pins, result)| {
                    let n_clusters = result.cluster_centers.len_of(Axis(0));
                    let mut groups: Vec<Vec<_>> = ::alloc::vec::from_elem(
                        Vec::new(),
                        n_clusters,
                    );
                    for (pin, &label) in clock_pins.iter().zip(result.labels.iter()) {
                        groups[label].push(pin.clone());
                    }
                    groups
                        .into_iter()
                        .map(|group_insts| {
                            let dis = MBFFG::cal_mean_dis(&group_insts);
                            (group_insts, dis)
                        })
                })
                .collect_vec();
            return clustered_instances_with_distance;
        }
        pub fn merging_kmeans(&mut self) {
            let mut clustered_instances_with_distance = self
                .group_clock_instances_by_kmeans(
                    self
                        .get_clock_groups()
                        .iter()
                        .map(|x| x.iter().map(|pin| pin.inst()).collect_vec())
                        .collect_vec(),
                );
            let grouped_dis_values = clustered_instances_with_distance
                .iter()
                .map(|x| x.1)
                .collect_vec();
